Dumergue Cabinet Overthrown After Only Nine Months in Power 80

Constitutional Reform Bill Was the Fatal Blow

Flandin Ordered to Form a New Cabinet

National Sentiment is Volatile; Paris is Under Strict Guard

[Paris] The Dumergue cabinet has recently resigned in its entirety. The reason is that Prime Minister Dumergue's proposed constitutional reform bill and the 1935 provisional budget bill were met with disagreement from the cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party, and all the parties of the extreme left in the House of Representatives and the Radical Socialist Party also expressed their opposition. Therefore, the "Party Truce" cabinet, which was established on February 9 of this year, was inevitably disintegrated. (Eighth Havas Dispatch)

[Paris] The Dumergue government, which had been in power for a full nine months, resigned today, which will once again set off a political storm in France. Dumergue had no choice but to step down because five cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party refused to withdraw their resignation letters. After President Lebrun accepted the cabinet's resignation, he immediately invited Laval, the leader of the right-center party, to form a new cabinet. Laval declined, so the president invited Flandin, a member of the right-center party and the current Minister of Public Works, to form a cabinet. Flandin accepted this task, and the president was relieved.

After a cabinet meeting this morning, Cabinet Minister Herriot, without portfolio, gave a typewritten copy of his resignation letter to the Prime Minister, along with the resignation letters of the Radical Party cabinet members, to a group of French journalists and foreign reporters waiting. The letter, four pages long, was signed by Herriot and Minister of Education Bertod, Minister of Aviation Perrin, and Minister of Agriculture Quilles. Minister of Commerce Laimolo and Mahchando were not named due to illness. The letter stated that the Radical Socialist cabinet members strictly adhered to the contract of party truce made when they joined the cabinet, but Prime Minister Dumergue recently wanted to implement various major political reforms without consulting them first, causing them to no longer be able to respect the conditions in the contract.

After receiving the letter, the Prime Minister consulted with other cabinet members and drafted a letter to the President, which severely criticized the selfishness of the Radical Socialist Party, and said that if the demands of the political group holding full power on February 6 (when riots broke out in Paris, causing the Daladier government to collapse and the Dumergue government to take over) were to be succumbed to, then the "truce" could no longer exist, and the government's decisions would all follow the party's pleasures, which was not possible.

Dumergue was warmly cheered by the public when he left the presidential palace for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and returned to the Prime Minister's Office today. He then left the palace with his wife. Dumergue issued a warning to the nation, saying, "I have been forced to resign. I now urge all citizens to remain calm and self-possessed, as this is necessary in order to find the best way to escape today's difficulties and for the sake of the country's interests."

Dumergue told reporters that some people in Congress were planning to overthrow the cabinet by taking advantage of the country's current financial insufficiency.

The new Prime Minister Flandin has held various important positions in the government since the European War, but this is the first time he has served as Prime Minister. (Eighth Reuters Telegraph)

[Paris] At the same time, national sentiment is very volatile. Yesterday, the Prime Minister was not noticed when he left the House of Representatives, which has aroused general comments. The authorities are now afraid that the riots in Paris on February 6 will be repeated, so they have stepped up security. The number of police on the streets has tripled, and the Grand Conservatory of Music has been converted into a temporary headquarters for the police. (Seventh Reuters Telegraph)

[Paris] The streets of Paris are now on alert, fearing a reaction after the Dumergue cabinet is overthrown. There are now car guards stationed in the Luxembourg Palace, and police are also stationed in the Senate and the surrounding streets. (Eighth Reuters Telegraph)

[Paris] At the State Council meeting this morning, four cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party (Cabinet Minister Herriot without portfolio, Minister of Education Bertod, Minister of Merchant Marine Pedron, and Minister of Agriculture Gueille) formally submitted their resignations to Prime Minister Dumergue. At 11:30 a.m., after the four resigning cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party left the meeting, Prime Minister Dumergue and his colleagues drafted the cabinet's resignation letter. Thus, the Party Truce cabinet was overthrown. As for the letter from the cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party to Prime Minister Dumergue, it first praised Dumergue's achievements, and then said that the nature of the constitutional reform bill proposed by the Prime Minister exceeded the scope of the Party Truce contract. In order to be loyal to their principles and obligations, they had to submit their resignations. A communiqué was issued when the State Council meeting closed, stating that the cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party could not agree on the provisional budget bill and submitted their resignations, so the cabinet submitted its resignation in its entirety.

The Dumergue cabinet was established on February 9 of this year, when the Daladier cabinet was overthrown due to bloody riots in Paris. Lebrun then ordered former President Dumergue to unite all parties except the extreme left to form a Party Truce cabinet. For nine months, the Dumergue cabinet rectified finances, reformed taxation, reduced government spending, and clarified the judiciary. The budget was balanced and the political situation gradually stabilized. Recently, Prime Minister Dumergue wanted to thoroughly rectify domestic affairs and enhance administrative power, so he advocated reforming the constitution. The constitutional reform bill had four main points: first, to enhance the administrative power neglected in the constitution; second, when a conflict occurs between the government and the two houses, if the House of Representatives has been elected for a full year, but with the consent of the President and the Prime Minister, it can be dissolved without the approval of the Senate; third, to ensure the service of legislative personnel, such as civil servants who disobey government actions, they may be dismissed. This constitutional reform bill was discussed at the Radical Socialist Party Congress in Lanté and passed a resolution, expressing support for enhancing administrative power, but opposing the dissolution of the parliament without the consent of the Senate. However, the Congress still granted the Radical Party cabinet members the right to freely express their views. Therefore, after the parliament reopened yesterday, Prime Minister Dumergue could have immediately submitted the constitutional reform bill, but amending the constitution requires a constitutional conference formed by the merger of the two houses for discussion. After the constitution is amended, dissolving the parliament and re-electing it will take a considerable amount of time. The next year's budget is approaching in the blink of an eye, and it is difficult to delay for a long time. Therefore, Prime Minister Dumergue planned to submit a provisional budget bill for January, February, and March of next year to the parliament, requesting its passage, and then continue to discuss the constitutional reform bill. However, the cabinet members of the Radical Socialist Party, in accordance with the resolution of the Lanté Congress, opposed the constitutional reform bill, so they could not agree on the submission of the provisional budget bill. Since the opinions of both sides were incompatible, the four cabinet members of the Radical Party submitted their resignations this morning. At this point, it was impossible for Prime Minister Dumergue to form a minority cabinet, and Dumergue had already stated yesterday that he did not want to request the Senate's consent to dissolve the parliament, because otherwise, public opinion would accuse him of intending to be a dictator. Therefore, Prime Minister Dumergue decided not to attend the House of Representatives this afternoon, and the cabinet submitted its resignation in its entirety to President Lebrun. (Eighth Reuters Telegraph)

[Paris] All efforts to avoid a cabinet crisis have now failed. Prime Minister Dumergue has also decided to step down. The most important question now is the maintenance of the "Party Truce." Since it is required by most newspapers, and the consolidation of public administration must continue, who is most suitable to take on this important task? This is what the general public urgently wants to know. Excisive News said, "Foreign countries are now watching us. Do not let them feel that we have divergent opinions on domestic affairs, because there are many people who take advantage of our infighting to find flaws. For the sake of the present, it is appropriate to show a calm attitude to the outside world. This is the highest obligation of the country and each individual." The Morning Post wrote, "From tonight onwards, a new all-party truce national unity cabinet should be formed again, so that those who spy on the country from abroad can distinguish the true face of France, and those who want to take advantage of the weaknesses of our country will all return in despair." (Eighth Havas Dispatch)

Under the Control of the Japanese Army, Sham Organizations Change Military Systems and Intensify Training 89

Eliminating Complex Elements for Utilization

Establishing Horse Breeding Farms to Increase Military Horses

Changchun Correspondence: The Japanese army, considering that the elements within the puppet army are complex and that without strict elimination and special training, they are insufficient for the Japanese army to drive, has since changing the military district, implemented the recruitment of new soldiers and the establishment of a new army. As for the reconstruction of military camps and the establishment of military horse breeding farms, they are all very active. The details are recorded as follows:

Measures for Recruiting New Soldiers: The Japanese ordered the puppet organization to change the military system, break the traditional private system, to prevent taking the opportunity to revolt. Since its implementation, the puppet army's senior military officers have been transferred separately. Now, in the name of refreshing the army, the old and incompetent elements are eliminated, and strong men are recruited. Regulations are formulated, and a semi-conscription system is tested. The Bao head, district head, and county head provide guarantees at each level, and those who have real estate, are between the ages of 18 and 25, are roughly literate, and are physically fit are qualified. The term of enlistment is temporarily set at two years. The Puppet First Military District Command has begun recruiting, with a total of seven locations in Fengcheng, Dihua, Linjiang, Yingkou, Shanchengzi, and Shenyang.

Puppet Review and Autumn Maneuvers: After the puppet military system was changed, all the puppet troops were nominally supervised by Puyi himself, and a large-scale autumn exercise was held. The exercise took place from October 13 for three days in Changchun, with the location being from Datun to Nanling. The soldiers were divided into the North and South armies. The North Army was the puppet "Fengtian Jing'an Army", and the South Army was troops drawn from Jilin and Heilongjiang. Each army had 2,500 men, with artillery covering infantry and cavalry combat. On the 15th, Puyi personally inspected the troops and held a military parade, with Yu Zhishan as the commander. In addition, the Puppet Ministry of Military Affairs, having changed the military system, and in order to boost the spirit of the army, summoned the commanders of 77 regiments of infantry and cavalry and gathered them at the Puppet Palace in Changchun on the anniversary of Japan's recognition of the puppet state of Manchuria (September 15). Puyi personally presented the military flags, granting each regiment a military flag, including infantry regiments 1 to 26, 33 to 35, cavalry regiments 4 to 32, 39 to 44, training infantry regiments 4 and 5, training cavalry regiments 4 and 5, and puppet Jing'an cavalry regiments 1 to 8, totaling 77 regiments.

Building Military Camps at the Dafosi Temple: The Puppet Ministry of Military Affairs previously designated the Dafosi Temple in Chengde City to be renovated into a military camp. The Yuji Construction Company has contracted for the renovation, and the work has been accelerated since construction began. It has now been completed and can accommodate more than 1,000 people.

Establishing Military Horse Breeding Farms: In order to improve and increase horses, the Puppet Ministry of Military Affairs established the puppet "National Horse Breeding Farm." In August, the official system of the puppet National Horse Breeding Farm was announced, and preparations were actively made. It is reported that it has been decided to establish two farms first: (1) the Hailar National Horse Breeding Farm, with jurisdiction over the Puppet Xing'an North Province and specific designated areas; (2) the Taonan National Horse Breeding Farm, with jurisdiction over Taonan, Anguang, Zhendong, Tuquan, Zhanyu, Kaitong, and other counties, as well as the Puppet Xing'an South Province and specific designated areas. (Northeast News Agency)

Rampant Banditry in Yutian 90

Bandits Rob in Broad Daylight in the City

Neighboring Counties Blockade to Prevent Bandits from Fleeing

Tianjin Correspondence: Banditry in various parts of eastern Luan has recently been most severe in Yutian. Just a dozen or so miles from the city, there are large and small groups of dozens to hundreds of bandits entrenched, looting in all directions during the day. The militia and police teams are overwhelmed with prevention and suppression. On the 3rd of this month, the Wang residence in Yutian South Gate was broken into by a gang of about 20 bandits in broad daylight and looted empty. Then they went to the adjacent Ye residence and looted countless valuables as well. The whole process lasted two hours. The security team of the war zone stationed in the city turned a blind eye and allowed them to plunder and flee far away. As a result, the upper classes of the city have moved away one after another to avoid banditry. The major towns of Yahong Bridge and Wangxiezhuang in Hongqiao Town outside the city have been looted dozens of times. The markets are deserted, and gatherings have stopped. Merchants have also transported bulky goods elsewhere. Wangxiezhuang was occupied by more than 200 bandits on the 4th of this month. The Yutian County Militia has been dispatched to suppress them. Zunhua, being adjacent to the county, has a duty to assist and has also sent police and militia to assist in the suppression. The militias of Zunhua, Qian'an, Fengrun, and Jixian, because of the large number of bandits in Yutian, are guarding against their intrusion and are all blocking the borders. In particular, Zunhua is facing enemies on both sides and must both guard against the bandits from Yanshankou outside the Great Wall and also consider the invasion of bandit gangs from Yutian. The militia is insufficient for deployment and defense. In order to defend themselves, the farmers have formed joint village associations. The 68 villages in the Mizi Camp in the Third District took the lead in forming an association a few days ago, gathering more than 500 village guards, with Wang Jizong as the commander for training. The weapons are all self-provided by the people. Other districts will also follow suit. It is said that the bandits in Yutian can be divided into three categories. The first category is purely bandits who are forced to make a living and seek to solve their current problems, accounting for about three tenths of the bandits in Yutian. The second category is the plainclothes teams of Liu Guitang and Shi Yousan, who have backgrounds, are between soldiers and bandits, and use saving the country as a slogan to carry out their robbery, accounting for about five tenths. The third category belongs to the Security Supplementary Team in the war zone. The team has not listened to the provincial order to reorganize from beginning to end, relying on Yutian being within the war zone, and the province cannot take decisive measures, so the relationship with Shi Yousan is still maintained. The team soldiers are in contact with the plainclothes teams. They are soldiers during the day and change into plain clothes to become bandits at night. Because guns and bullets are readily available, it is very easy to carry out robbery. This accounts for about two tenths of the total number of bandits in Yutian. Yutian is disturbed by these three categories of bandits, and the local area is unsettled, the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted. Ba County is the hardest hit. Because the police and militia teams of Fengrun, Jixian, Zunhua, and Qian'an are still quite strong, and the border areas are strictly guarded, the bandits cannot cross over. The strength of the Ba County regiment police is weak, and because the Jiyun Canal in the county has overflowed after the water rose, and has not fallen until now, four districts of the county are a vast expanse of water, making transportation inconvenient. The bandits take advantage of the boats to intercept and rob. County Magistrate Zhao of Ba County has been planning to expand the police regiment and install long-distance telephone projects, preparing to clear the bandits in the territory during the winter defense period. In addition to the semi-official bandits in Yutian, who must wait for the War Zone Clearance Committee to be responsible for handling them, the newly appointed County Magistrate Huang Zhongkai is planning to gather the police regiment and increase the suppression of the pure bandits. (6th)

Guangdong Province's Budget for the 23rd Year 91

Income Does Not Cover Expenditures by More Than 26 Million

Changing Grain Tax to Land Tax to Be Implemented Soon

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province's finances have recently been burdened by heavy expenditures, and the budget for the 23rd year is in a situation where income does not cover expenditures. The authorities ordered the provincial government to order all agencies that, in the future, all directly productive agencies should continue to spend as before, but indirectly productive agencies should strive to reduce and conserve. According to the report on the total amount of income and expenditures for the 23rd year made by the Financial Commissioner's Office, the total budgeted income part of the year is 43,446,204.40 yuan. According to the 70% standard of the income in the 22nd year, the actual income is 31,715,729.22 yuan. The expenditure part is statistically 58,400,347.12 yuan. The income and expenditures do not cover 26,687,617.91 yuan. According to the authorities, in terms of donations and taxes, more than 80 kinds of harsh and miscellaneous taxes and donations were abolished before August 1 this year, resulting in a reduction of more than 4.7 million yuan per year. It is planned to abolish more than 40 kinds next year, resulting in a reduction of more than 1.6 million yuan per year. A total of more than 120 kinds have been abolished or scheduled to be abolished, resulting in a reduction of more than 6.4 million yuan per year. As for the item of increasing revenue, the change from grain tax to land tax throughout the province is being actively carried out. The investigation of farmland in each county will be completed one after another. The change to land tax can be implemented in the short term. In terms of the provincial treasury, the previous allocation of grain tax in each county was "80% allocated to the provincial treasury, 20% retained in the county" as local political expenses. If the land tax is changed, 50% can be allocated and 50% retained, and the government revenue will increase instead. This is because there is no bad habit of cheating on grain tax. In the past, the income from grain tax was only 60% to 70%. The accumulated abuses included "land without tax" and "tax without land". After changing to land tax, there will be no such abuses. The income of the local government in the county will also be relatively abundant. In the past, 20% of the grain tax was retained in the county, but now it is 50%. If so, the county's political expenses will increase, and the construction, education, and security expenses at the local level will not be as stretched as before. (November 3)

Records of a Northwestern Inspection 92

— Our Special Correspondent, Geng Ya

The Scenery of Anxi County

In the Spring and Autumn period, Anxi was the land of the Western Rong. The Yuezhi Rong of Qin resided there. During the Han dynasty, it was part of the Dunhuang Commandery, governing six counties, and was one of the four commanderies of the Hexi Corridor. The city was built in the sixth year of the Yongzheng reign of the Qing Dynasty. It has a circumference of six li and seven fen, with open spaces at the four corners. Only around the Drum Tower and the east and west streets is there a concentration of population, occupying about one-sixth of the city's area. The desolate situation can be imagined. The county extends 580 li from east to west and over 500 li from north to south. This only refers to the more populated areas. If the vast, deserted lands to the north and south are included, the total area of the county exceeds ten thousand square li. It is 360 li northwest to Xingxing Gorge on the border of Hami, and extending to Hami, it is 880 li, all of which is Gobi desert. It is 250 li southeast to the Sandaogou on the border of Yumen. There are many ditches. Extending further to Lanzhou, it is 2,160 li, and to Nanjing, it is several thousand li. It is 130 li west to Shuang Dunzi, west of Luchao Gou on the border of Dunhuang, near the fields, which are prone to flooding. The facilities at each post station, during the Yongzheng period of the Qing Dynasty, included six horses per station and three grooms. Each horse was provided with 8.5 fen of silver for fodder daily, and each groom received one tael of silver per month for wages and five dou of grain. In the early Republic, the old stations were abolished and replaced with postal services. For Gobi stations where postal routes were not established, laborers were still hired to guard the wells and springs, receiving two or three dou of wheat per month.

The geology consists of the Mazong Mountain in the north and the Qilian Mountain in the south, both of which are igneous rock. In between lies a plain, cultivated for farmland. The land in Wuying and the various trenches, namely Nanbei Gong, Tashi, and the Third, Fourth, and Fifth trenches (all of which are village names), is loamy soil. Qiaozi, Bulongji, Dongbatou, etc., all have alkaline soil, and the rest is Gobi Desert. Fortunately, the water table is not very deep. The climate has a coldest period of about 90 days per year and a hottest period of 50 days. Rainfall is minimal, and winter snow and autumn dew are rare (the snow on the southern mountains never melts). The summer sun is scorching, and the winter is severely cold. In the spring and winter, there are particularly violent winds, with sand and gravel flying, darkening the sky and lasting for days. They uproot trees and destroy houses, causing great harm. In the past, the winds of Anxi, the cold of Zhenxi, and the heat of Turpan were known as the "Three Absolutes."

The Southern Mountain is fifty li south of the city, starting from Shuangtabao, called Luanshanzi, and extending west to Guazhou Kou, called Jieshanzi. It is mostly dark green and black stone, without water, and no grass or trees grow. There are occasional coal mines. West to Dunhuang, it turns into quicksand. This mountain stretches across the county for about 200 li, with peaks only a hundred feet high. The Snow Mountain is three hundred li south of the county, which is the Qilian Peak, over eight thousand feet high. The mountains are covered in snow, which melts slightly in the spring and summer, providing water for cultivation. It is rich in various metals and sulfur, but it is occupied by the Qing Fan (a term for local ethnic groups) and has never been mined. The Salt Lake is eighty li south of the city. Natural salt blocks can be dug freely. Transported to the city, they sell for only one or two copper coins per catty. Pu Cheng Mountain is 580 li north of the county and is rich in lead and silver deposits. It was mined in the past but was abandoned due to unrest. Da Qingshan produces Cistanche deserticola and Cynomorium songaricum. Licorice is everywhere. Locals cut the branches for firewood, and the thick roots, as thick as a fist, are used for medicine. Other products such as rhubarb, Lycium chinense, and Ephedra sinica are also abundant. The animal and livestock resources are complete. Wild animals include gazelles, wild foxes, badgers, wild rabbits, jackals, leopards, lynx, wild horses, deer, musk deer, etc. Apart from rice, all crops are grown. Melons and fruits come from Dunhuang.

One hundred and sixty li south of the city is the Yulin Grottoes. Springs come from both mountains and never dry up in all four seasons. Tall trees and abundant grass cover about forty or fifty li. Inside there is a large Buddha statue, sixteen zhang tall, with golden colors shining brightly, magnificent and solemn. The other Buddha caves also have many statues, said to be from the Western Xia Dynasty, later renovated by the Tang and Yuan dynasties. Also in this mountain is an ivory Buddha statue, the size of a palm, two pieces joined together, with a Manjushri Buddha image carved on the outside and countless small Buddhas carved on the inside, exquisite and intricate, resembling Indian carvings. It is undoubtedly an offering from a Tibetan monk of the Tang Dynasty. It is said that this Buddha is a sacred object to suppress the land and ensure peace. During the Tongzhi Rebellion, it flew away without wings, and the mountain spring suddenly dried up. Later, two or three thousand taels of silver were spent until the Guangxu period to find and return the original object. The spring water then flowed again, which can be called the ultimate in mythological ability. This Buddha is now treasured in rotation by local gentry. If one wants to borrow it, the city gentry entrust it to the village gentry, and the village gentry push it back to the city gentry. Therefore, the previous Northwestern Scientific Expedition and all past county magistrates wanted to feast their eyes on it but failed to do so. If this object is as precious and rare as described above, it should be properly preserved to avoid the fate of the ancient scriptures of Dunhuang, which were stolen by foreigners.

As for the ancient relics in the city, the first is a deep spring under the Drum Tower. Legend has it that "the spring is very strong, secretly connected to the Sule River north of the city. In the past, a geomancer said that Anxi would produce an official who would be rebellious and unfavorable to the border. If this spring were blocked, its feng shui could be broken." Later, it was covered with seven pots, and four wells were dug in four directions three or four zhang away to divert its source. Since then, although the spring still gushes out, its power has been greatly reduced. The deep spring is made into a well with stone, about ten feet deep. A wooden railing surrounds the well, three feet square at the bottom and about five feet high, with a door opening to the north for drawing water. A pillar stands on the railing, piercing the center of the Drum Tower's bottom surface, with two dragons coiling on it, opening their mouths and waving their claws, as if trying to enter the well. In addition, the two wells in the northeast have been filled in, and the two wells in the southwest are still used for drinking. However, residents compete to draw water from the deep spring for boiling opium, as it is said to filter the impurities and have a clear fragrance. The Drum Tower is over two zhang high and forty steps square, with eight-step-wide arches. There is a well in the center, and vegetable stalls are set up in the four arches, which hinders traffic and the view. The upper pavilion has long collapsed. South of the tower, leaning against the wall, is a Mingchi Building, as tall as the Drum Tower. Although it bears the sign of the Education Hall, it has been rented out as a shop. The current county magistrate, Xie Dousheng, upon taking office, seeing that the deep spring and the Drum Tower are the only historical sites in Anxi, plans to move the Mingchi Building to the top of the Drum Tower, add some repairs, and convert it into a public education hall. However, local funds are scarce, and implementation remains to be seen.

There is a river to the north of the city and a canal to the south. Digging five feet deep reveals a water source. The soil is fertile and suitable for cultivation. Willows and elaeagnus angustifolia are lush and verdant, stretching for dozens of li. Looking out from a height, one feels especially pleased. About five li south of the city, there is an ancient fortress, thought to have been a military camp that was abandoned. The north and south walls of the fortress have not collapsed much. The east and west sides have been blown by strong winds and are fragmented, resembling city battlements, and some are almost submerged by quicksand. Also, the south gate of Anxi and the inner walls of the east city are now blocked by quicksand. The east-west winds in Anxi are stronger than the north-south winds. When they come, they always carry fine sand. When they encounter city buildings, trees, or forests, they are slightly hindered, and the sand falls down, accumulating like sand dunes. It is said that the old barrier wall outside the east gate was once lively with residents but was buried by quicksand due to the lack of trees. Therefore, to reduce the disaster of wind and sand, planting forests extensively is essential. The water table in Anxi is shallow and abundant, making it easy to grow trees. For fields lacking canal water, wells can be dug for irrigation (various counties in Shandong benefit greatly from using well water to irrigate the fields). Local people, please do not neglect this.

Songjiang 93

Land Bureau to be Established on a Fixed Date

Our county previously received provincial orders to actively carry out land survey work, and the county magistrate was appointed as the preparatory member of the Land Bureau, to first engage in household land surveying. Later, the county magistrate resigned from his concurrent position, and Zhu Tongqi was appointed as the preparatory member in his place, with the office attached to the county government. Preparations have been completed, and it is scheduled to be officially established on the 11th of this month, with the bureau located at the First Building. The provincial government appointed Zhu, the preparatory member, as the director of the bureau. It is heard that the bureau will be divided into three sections, with a technical officer and employees also appointed. As for the internal staff, except for the head of the First Section, who will be concurrently held by the director, and the head of the Second Section, who will be concurrently held by the head of the land survey team, the rest have been largely decided internally.

Water Patrol Team Captures Suspected Thieves

The home of Zhong Yuping, located at Taipailou in our city, was suddenly broken into by four robbers carrying submachine guns and bayonets on the evening of the previous day. They gained entry by pretending to deliver a gift, tied up the victim, imprisoned him in a room, and stole over three hundred yuan in foreign currency, as well as gold jewelry and antiques. That night, special agents and security teams from the Public Security Bureau intercepted them from all sides but did not find them overnight. This case has attracted much attention from the military and police. The Water Patrol Team discovered a man named Qi Jingen (nickname Ata) behaving improperly at Jiangjing Bridge in our city, suspected him of being involved, and arrested him. The team investigated him. It is heard that Qi Jingen denies any involvement in the Zhong surname robbery and has permission to seek bail.

Kunshan 94

Chairman Lin Visits Kunshan for Sightseeing

Lin Sen, Chairman of the National Government, and Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, arrived at the Qingyang Port Garden Hotel by express train from Shanghai at 9:00 AM on the 8th to visit the Chrysanthemum Exhibition of the two roads. Upon hearing the news, leaders of various agencies in our county gathered to welcome them at Qingyang. At about 10:00 AM, Mr. Lin took a steamboat to the North Gate and climbed Ma'anshan to visit various scenic spots. At noon, he attended a public banquet hosted by various agencies at Ban Jian Yuan. After the banquet, Mayor Wu returned to Shanghai by express train at 1:30 PM. Chairman Lin took the Jingzha train back to Nanjing at 2:22 PM. Representatives from all sectors went to the station to see him off respectfully.

Disaster-Stricken Farmers Report Crop Failure to the County

Since the beginning of summer, Kunshan County has been plagued by drought. After surveying by the heads of various districts and townships, the total area of ​​disaster-stricken fields with no harvest is 111,708 mu. After the county reported the crop failure to the province, the county government was ordered to reject it and even increase taxes. Although various local public groups wired the province to argue for relief, there was no solution. At 10:00 AM on the 8th, over three thousand disaster-stricken farmers gathered at the East Gate and Da Xi Men, holding rice crops with no grains, and reported the crop failure to the county government, demanding the removal of disaster-stricken fields. County Magistrate Peng went to welcome Chairman Lin at the time. Section Chief Mei came out to comfort them with kind words and promised to report to higher authorities. The villagers then dispersed.

Wuxi 95

Employee of Bank of China Commits Suicide

Xu Zhenxia, ​​an employee of the Bank of China in our county, a 29-year-old from Suzhou, was the beloved son-in-law of the bank's director, Wu Zhihe. Xu's father, Weigan, was the director of the Agricultural and Industrial Bank in Hankou, and his uncle, Weizhen, was the director of the China Bank office in Changzhou. He had two younger brothers, Kuangxia and Qixia, who worked in the Bank of China in Suzhou and Shanghai, respectively. Zhenxia loved Peking opera and was skilled in writing. He was also a special contributor to the Shanghai Saturday Weekly, the Coral Magazine edited by Fan Yanqiao, and the Mingjing supplement of the Suzhou Ming Bao, under the pen names Juanhun and Juanyun. Seven years ago, Zhenxia's wife (Wu Zhihe's eldest daughter) passed away due to childbirth, and Zhenxia was always depressed. During his spare time after work, he would often go to the director's office to chat with his father-in-law, vaguely revealing his intention to marry his wife's younger sister. Wu's second daughter, Jin Hui, who is currently studying at Shanghai Tongde Medical School, is 29 years old and has both talent and beauty. However, Wu sternly refused. Zhenxia was disappointed that his request was hopeless, and his depression worsened. The night before, Xu was talking and laughing with his colleagues as usual, showing no signs of anything unusual. Unexpectedly, after returning to his dormitory to sleep, he had not arrived at the office by about 9:00 AM the next morning. The office staff went upstairs to wake him up and found the doors tightly closed. They knocked but received no response. When they peeked through the crack, they saw Zhenxia's neck tied with a trouser belt, cushioned with a towel, hanging himself by the door. They immediately reported to the director and broke down the door to enter and untie him, using artificial respiration to resuscitate him, but to no avail. They then requested Chinese and Western doctors such as Zhou Lun and Xu Songquan to provide emergency treatment, but it was too late to revive him. Director Wu has urgently telegraphed his family members to come to Wuxi to handle the funeral arrangements. However, the bank has kept it a secret from the outside world. The police investigation has also found no clues.

Agricultural Warehouse Rice Mortgage Measures

For the purpose of rescuing farmers and regulating rural finance, Wuxi Farmers Bank is planning to establish rural warehouses and agricultural product transportation offices, and the provincial bank has appointed Zou Hanxiang as the director of the Wuxi Transportation Office. In view of the severe drought this year, the Yangtze River Basin, known as the richest rice-producing area in Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, and other provinces, has suffered poor harvests, and there are even discussions about restricting exports. Even in Wuxi, the harvest is at most less than 60% of last year's. The lack of food next year is already foreseeable. Yesterday, the Agricultural Warehouse Committee was convened to discuss remedial measures, deciding to jointly establish 22 agricultural warehouses in the four rural areas with the Farmers Bank and the pawnshop trade association and passing the following measures: (1) Farmers Bank will operate warehouses independently at Dongting, Qianqiao, and Anzhen; (2) Each pawnshop acts as an agent of the agricultural warehouse at these locations: Qingming Bridge Shangtang, Youxiatang, Zhouxin Town, Nanqiao, Yanqiao, Changan Bridge, Bashi Bridge, Zhangjing Bridge, Yanjia Bridge, Meicun, Dangkou, Houzhai Town, Huadafang Village, Yuqi Town, Qianzhou, Yangshuyuan, Fengzhuang, Hudai, Yangjian Town, and 19 pawnshops; (3) The monthly interest on the loan is 1.5%, and the pawnshop agent charges 1.6%; (4) Each household must mortgage at least 5 dou and at most 10 shi of rice; (5) The mortgaged rice is calculated at 70% of the market price; (6) All warehouse mortgages start from December 1st. Also, the rice trade association, fearing that the Farmers Bank's operation of warehouses and transportation offices would affect the industry, declared its opposition. The Chamber of Commerce has been mediating. Yesterday (the 8th), the Chamber of Commerce convened the Farmers Bank and rice bean industry in the afternoon to negotiate. Both sides have thoroughly understood each other, and the rice industry has also agreed to improve its business policies to converge.

Changzhou 96

Relief Representatives from Jin Province Return to Changzhou

Wujin County suffered a severe drought this year. The provincial government previously allocated 20,000 yuan for drought relief, but the county government planned to use 120,000 yuan for dredging rivers with relief work. In addition to raising half of the amount locally, the provincial government must allocate at least 40,000 yuan or more, otherwise, it will not be enough to allocate. Shi Ziquan, the third section chief of the county government, previously went to Jin Province to fight for relief, but there were no results. Fellow villagers of Wujin living in Beijing held a meeting to discuss. In addition to Wu Zhihui writing to the chairman in his private capacity, requesting an increase in relief funds, they also appointed representatives Cheng Cangbo, Yang Bingquan, and Wu Jingyu to arrive in Zhen on the 5th. Wujin also appointed representatives Gao Bozhen, Chen Dayou, and Wu Jingyuan to arrive in Zhen on the same day. They went to the provincial government together on the morning of the 6th. The provincial government committee meeting had just ended. Chairman Chen received them. Zhao, the Director of the Finance Department, Yu, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, and Shen, the Director of the Construction Department, were also present. Each representative stated three points: 1. Please allocate relief funds. Chairman Chen replied that it was difficult to increase the overall budget. 2. Autumn survey issue: Please exempt the grain tax on fields with no harvest and implement a general reduction for the rest. Director Zhao of the Finance Department expressed his acceptance. 3. Please return the 35,000 yuan of Wujin governance public bonds borrowed from various counties in Jiangbei to be used for relief work. Director Shen of the Construction Department said that the money owed by various counties in Jiangbei has only been collected by 10%, so it is impossible to allocate it at this time, so nothing was obtained. Each representative then returned to Changzhou, and the representatives living in Beijing returned to Beijing. It is heard that the issue of relief work still needs to be discussed further.

Jingjiang 97

Construction of New Prison Completed

The county government previously found that the prison was dilapidated, making defense unreliable, and the overcrowding made hygiene non-compliant. Therefore, it submitted an application to the High Court to raise funds and build a new prison. The work has been underway for two months. Now, all the projects have been completed and are in compliance with the original regulations. However, it is necessary to request the High Court to send personnel for inspection and acceptance to complete the procedure.

Yangzhou 98

Bandits Kidnap and Injure People in Western Suburbs

The home of Jiang Fengting, a farmer from the Xujiaxiang village in the second township of Yishu, Yangzhou County, was suddenly broken into by many bandits armed with guns the night before. They forbade them from making a sound and immediately searched and looted clothes. Jiang's abdomen was shot by a bandit and he fell to the ground unconscious. When the bandits left, they kidnapped Jiang Fengting's ten-year-old child. At Yingwankou, the child suddenly cried for help, which was discovered by the villagers, who gathered a crowd, rescued the child, and captured a bandit named Li Xian'gen. The remaining bandits escaped. The villagers sent the bandit and the hostage to the Xupuqiao Security Detachment in Yishu, and the team then captured a suspect named Cao Yuanju in Yuetangji. As for Jiang Fengting, the injured victim, he died on the 6th due to his serious injuries.

Murderer of Adulterer Surrenders Himself

Wang Juchang, the manager of the Shuangguiquan bathhouse in Touxiang in our city, found his wife, Wu, sleeping with Chen Juyuan, a worker in the shop, and killed him with an axe. Afterwards, Wang fled to evade punishment. Zhu, the prosecutor of the Jiangdu Court Prosecutor's Office, verified the facts and issued a warrant for the arrest of the murderer and summoned the bathhouse workers for interrogation. It is now known that Wang Juchang hid elsewhere after the crime. On the one hand, he asked people to intercede with the victim (the wife of the deceased) to ask for money to settle the matter. Later, because the District Procuratorate was investigating urgently and repeatedly summoned workers for questioning, Wang feared implicating the innocent and surrendered himself to the court. After several interrogations by the District Procuratorate, Wang confessed without denial. Yesterday, the court filed a lawsuit with the criminal court on the charge of causing death by injury.

Haimen 99

Dahua Company's Poison Pill Case

The Dahua Automobile Company on the newly opened Henan River in the county city was searched by County Magistrate Chen in person, along with police, the night before (the 5th) for selling ginseng and velvet antler and Anran opium-quitting pills containing toxic substances. A cylinder of white powder and playing cards were found. Shi Xunfu, the accountant, and Gu Weicheng, Lu Yongqing, and Ni Mingqi, the drivers, and ten other people were taken to the county for interrogation. According to Shi and Gu, Bao Jintang, the patrol captain of the Public Security Bureau, and Shen Zhongxiu, the driver of Qilin Town, also sold on their behalf. County Magistrate Chen ordered the police to arrest Bao Jintang and Shen Zhongxiu and send them to the county. Yesterday (the 6th), the trial continued. Bao and Shen confessed without denial. The court ordered that Shi, Gu, Bao, and Shen be detained together, and Lu Yongqing and the other eight people were released. It is heard that they will be sent to the Nantong Headquarters for interrogation in the next few days.

Nantong 100

Male and Female Drug Dealers Sentenced to Firing Squad

The Rugao County Government arrested Zhang Xikang and Zhang Wangshi, male and female drug dealers, and sent them to the Fourth District Security Command for interrogation. They were approved by the Nanchang Camp and brought back from the Rugao Police Team on the 7th to be executed by firing squad on the spot.

Water Police Team Suppresses Pirates

Qiu Xiangfeng, the captain of the Provincial Water Police Team, sent a telegram to the Fourth District Security Command reporting the progress of suppressing pirates in the Lvsi waters in recent days, stating that in this general attack, two large and small pirate ships were intercepted, eleven hostages were rescued, and more than twenty pirates were killed. The only injuries sustained by our team were to the captain and two attendants. They have returned to Tong for treatment. The rest of the team has been temporarily ordered to be led by He Yuanxin, the captain of the Second Detachment, and concentrated in Lvsi to await orders. The captured pirate ships and hostages have been handed over to the Lvsi District Office and the Fisheries Association for temporary custody, pending orders for verification and handling.

Funing 101

Section Chief and Engineer Robbed by Bandits

Zhou Yuchang, the third section chief of the Funing County Government, and Zhou Chenglian, an engineer, went to Beixiang Qitao to survey the Yellow River boundary line. They returned to the city yesterday, but unexpectedly, at about 4:00 PM, they passed through Sunzhuang Zhangzhuang when two bandits suddenly appeared, each holding a box gun, and dragged Zhou et al. to the north of the Yellow River. It was already midnight. They also wanted to shoot them to death. Zhou et al. had no choice but to hand over their clothes, foreign glasses, gold rings, and other items to the bandits. The bandits searched Zhou et al. for anything else, and then released them. They only escaped back to the county government today.

Jiashan 102

Bandits Kidnap and Injure People

Zhang Laochun, a resident of Shuangyu Village in Fengjing Town, is a well-to-do family with two sons, the eldest Daguan and the youngest Xiaoguan, who are not yet married. He has engaged a Zhou woman for the upcoming wedding next month. Last night, more than twenty bandits suddenly arrived, armed with wooden-shell guns and broadswords, broke into the house, and forbade them from making a sound, washing and looting property. On the verge of leaving, a bandit stabbed Daguan in the side with a knife, and blood flowed all over the ground. Xiaoguan was kidnapped, and the bandits demanded a thousand gold pieces for ransom. After checking the losses, it was found that 57 yuan in silver dollars and several pieces of gold jewelry were robbed.

Ningbo 103

Road Workers Assault and Injure Militiamen

During a play performed for a god's birthday celebration at the Huabaodian in the Fourth Gate of Yuyao, a certain Jia, a road worker from the Caojiu section of Guancao Road, was criticized by the audience for harassing women. The road worker, ashamed and angry, gathered forty to fifty road workers, each carrying kitchen knives, iron rakes, carrying poles, and other objects, and came to retaliate. For a time, the sound of people was noisy and the order was disrupted. The local security team heard the police and rushed to suppress it, but many people were beaten and injured. One person was stabbed in the throat with a kitchen knife, and one person's head was bleeding profusely. The injuries were the most serious. Later, the city-based main force team captured ten perpetrators, including Li Ayu, Wang Youfa, Wu Ruichang, Sun Canyong, and Lü Guocan, and took them in for interrogation.

Xiaoshan 104

Farmers Request Reduction or Exemption of Land Rent Due to Disaster

Since the beginning of summer, Nansha, Xiaoshan, has experienced a long drought with no rain. The cotton harvest in each township has varied due to this. However, soybeans and green beans have been greatly affected. In recent days, about 500 sand farmers from the sixth and seventh districts have gone to the county to report the crop failure and request rent exemption. Their intention is to not stop until their goal is achieved. Therefore, it is feared that land rent will be difficult to obtain as desired. As for the field rent, more than 50 townships in the east township have also reported to the county government requesting that personnel be sent to survey the disaster and notify the owners to estimate the damage in the fields within seven days.

Hangzhou 105

Patrol Boat Policeman Tragically Drowns

Yang Desheng, a member of the patrol team of the patrol boat of the Military Police Inspection Office of the Hangzhou Garrison Headquarters, was 26 years old and diligent in his service. The night before, he was standing guard on the bow of the ship, patrolling the Hangfu River with his gun and ammunition. It was late at night and dark. He was careless and accidentally fell into the water. Because he was carrying a rifle and a hundred rounds of ammunition, he sank to the bottom of the river due to the weight. The ship immediately stopped to rescue him, but it was difficult to rescue him in the dark. It was only yesterday that the body was recovered, which was a tragic sight.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Joint Silk Factory to be Established

The Jiangsu and Zhejiang Joint Silk Factory, since the National Economic Council Silk Improvement Association Organization Steering Committee began preparations, has had six companies in Zhejiang joining: Hangzhou, Kaiyuan, Qingyun, Huilun, Weicheng, and Heji. Eleven companies in Jiangsu have joined: Yongtai, Huaxing, and Ruilun. Xue Shouxuan, the chairman of the Steering Committee, convened representatives from silk factories in the two provinces to meet in Shanghai to discuss progress, so that it can be established next month. It is learned that the Silkworm Seed Industry and United Silk Factory Steering Committees of the Silkworm Association held a joint meeting yesterday and decided to issue a total of 1.2 million silkworm seeds in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces next spring. In addition to purchasing 500 new-style silk reeling machines in Shanghai to lease to various factories, another 500 machines will be purchased, with the expenses shared equally by the association and the factories.

Hefei 106

Joint Mining and Railway Project of Huainan Road is Completed

The joint mining and railway project of Huainan Coal Mine has been under construction for several months. The earthwork project and construction have been completed. The laying of sleepers and steel bones for sixty to seventy li has now begun and it is decided to open the line to traffic this year. As for the farmland occupied along the way, the price of farmland within Hefei is paid by the Dongwai Engineering Office, and within Dingyuan and Shou counties, it is paid by the county governments of those two counties. Payment has now begun in accordance with the regulations. As for the coal transported from the mine through the Luo River, two self-provided ships and rented civilian ships were used in the past. Now, because they are insufficient for use, ten iron barges have been purchased from Wuxi and are now in the Luo River for use. In anticipation of the opening of the mine to the Hefei railway section in a few days, a notice has been issued in Hefei to recruit twenty road police officers.

Hangzhou 111

Patrol Boat Policeman Tragically Drowns

Yang Desheng, a member of the patrol team of the patrol boat of the Military Police Inspection Office of the Hangzhou Garrison Headquarters, was 26 years old and diligent in his service. The night before, he was standing guard on the bow of the ship, patrolling the Hangfu River with his gun and ammunition. It was late at night and dark. He was careless and accidentally fell into the water. Because he was carrying a rifle and a hundred rounds of ammunition, he sank to the bottom of the river due to the weight. The ship immediately stopped to rescue him, but it was difficult to rescue him in the dark. It was only yesterday that the body was recovered, which was a tragic sight.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Joint Silk Factory to be Established

The Jiangsu and Zhejiang Joint Silk Factory, since the National Economic Council Silk Improvement Association Organization Steering Committee began preparations, has had six companies in Zhejiang joining: Hangzhou, Kaiyuan, Qingyun, Huilun, Weicheng, and Heji. Eleven companies in Jiangsu have joined: Yongtai, Huaxing, and Ruilun. Xue Shouxuan, the chairman of the Steering Committee, convened representatives from silk factories in the two provinces to meet in Shanghai to discuss progress, so that it can be established next month. It is learned that the Silkworm Seed Industry and United Silk Factory Steering Committees of the Silkworm Association held a joint meeting yesterday and decided to issue a total of 1.2 million silkworm seeds in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces next spring. In addition to purchasing 500 new-style silk reeling machines in Shanghai to lease to various factories, another 500 machines will be purchased, with the expenses shared equally by the association and the factories.

Hefei 112

Joint Mining and Railway Project of Huainan Road is Completed

The joint mining and railway project of Huainan Coal Mine has been under construction for several months. The earthwork project and construction have been completed. The laying of sleepers and steel bones for sixty to seventy li has now begun and it is decided to open the line to traffic this year. As for the farmland occupied along the way, the price of farmland within Hefei is paid by the Dongwai Engineering Office, and within Dingyuan and Shou counties, it is paid by the county governments of those two counties. Payment has now begun in accordance with the regulations. As for the coal transported from the mine through the Luo River, two self-provided ships and rented civilian ships were used in the past. Now, because they are insufficient for use, ten iron barges have been purchased from Wuxi and are now in the Luo River for use. In anticipation of the opening of the mine to the Hefei railway section in a few days, a notice has been issued in Hefei to recruit twenty road police officers.

Zhu Xuetian's Letter 113

Respected Editor,

I have just read your newspaper and noticed a section on the Baoshan Party Affairs Dispute. This is inconsistent with the facts. The Baoshan Party affairs have been well managed for a long time and there are no disputes. Before me, Xuetian was the head of the Baoshan Urban-Rural Public Education Center for a year and a half and was repeatedly commended by the educational authorities. In August of this year, Xuetian was ordered to go to the central government for training. The Education Bureau ignored the facts and dismissed Xuetian with the words "ineffective work." However, a week after the dismissal, Xuetian received an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, commending him for his excellent performance. At the Jiangsu Provincial Government banquet a few days ago, Xuetian also reported this matter in detail. Chairman Chen and the heads of various departments, as well as the members of the Provincial Party Headquarters, all found it strange and regrettable. Xuetian is now serving in Yutang, and his future actions will be determined by the Party and the country. The report in your newspaper is obviously a rumor intended to confuse public opinion. I am writing this special letter to correct this. Please publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section. I would be eternally grateful.

Sincerely,

Zhu Xuetian

November 7th

Chairman Lin Returned to Nanjing Yesterday Morning 114

Stopped by Qingyang Port to View Chrysanthemums

Mayor Wu Accompanied Him Before Returning to Shanghai

The Qingyang Port Chrysanthemum Exhibition held by the Shanghai-Nanjing-Ningbo Railway Administration has been attracting a constant stream of visitors since its opening on November 3rd. Chairman Lin of the National Government, taking advantage of his return trip to Nanjing from Shanghai, also stopped by to see it. Yesterday morning at 7:30 AM, Mr. Lin, accompanied by Shanghai Mayor Wu, Secretary Guo, Land Bureau Director Jin, and the famous Shanghai doctor Lu Zhong'an, arrived at the North Station. They were received by Deputy Director Wu Shaozeng of the Railway Administration, Chief of General Affairs Xu Yuanfang, Deputy Chief Cao Shengzhi, Chief of Transportation Xiao Weiguo, Chief of Materials Mo Heng, and Police Chief Ma Shaoping. They were escorted into a specially decorated private car. The Municipal Government sent a military band to the station to bid them farewell. At 8:00 AM, the train headed west amidst the melodious music. Around 9:00 AM, they arrived at Qingyang Port, where Kunshan County Magistrate Peng Baichuan welcomed them at the station. They went to the Railway Garden Hotel to rest briefly upstairs. The room displayed several of the most famous and valuable chrysanthemums from Shanghai. Chairman Lin immediately wrote the horizontal inscription "Lasting Fragrance in Old Age" and inscribed on a calligraphy album "Eastern Fence Autumn Beauty," signing it "Qingzhi Elderly." Mayor Wu wrote the horizontal inscription "Great Autumn Scenery" and inscribed the four characters "Pine and Chrysanthemum Still Exist" on a calligraphy album. Afterwards, they went downstairs, where Deputy Director Wu led them on a tour of the chrysanthemums displayed throughout the garden. At 10:30 AM, the guests and hosts took a group photo to commemorate the occasion. Then, at Magistrate Peng's invitation, they took a speedboat to visit Yufeng Mountain in Kunshan. Deputy Director Wu, Chief Xu, and Chief Wang of the Transportation Department of the Railway Administration accompanied them. In the afternoon, Chairman Lin took a train to Nanjing from Kunshan. Mayor Wu and others returned directly to Shanghai from Kunshan. The weather was mild and the autumn scenery was beautiful. Many people from various places continued to visit the Qingyang Port Chrysanthemum Exhibition.

National Federation of Commerce Urges Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Conclude Sino-French-Vietnamese Treaty 116

Overseas Chinese Eagerly Await Reduction of Import Tariffs on Chinese Goods in Vietnam

The National Federation of Commerce yesterday submitted a petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to urge the conclusion of the Sino-French-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty. The petition stated: "To the esteemed Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, we have received a joint letter from the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Southern Vietnam and the Overseas Chinese Association for Promoting the Sino-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty, requesting that we forward their appeal for the conclusion of the Sino-French-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty. Aside from the original documents on file, we will not repeat them. However, it is stated at the end: 'The industry and commerce of overseas Chinese in Vietnam are in a desperate situation. The only hope lies in the implementation of the Sino-French Commercial Treaty, reducing tariffs on Chinese goods and improving the treatment of overseas Chinese. Therefore, they are struggling to survive, awaiting a change in the situation.' We respectfully request that you urgently negotiate with France to reduce the tariffs on Chinese goods entering Vietnam. For goods that previously enjoyed special preferential tariff rates, we request that they be restored. For other Chinese goods, we request that they receive the most favored nation tariff rate.' We have approved this. This case has been repeatedly reported and urged by affiliated associations. The Sino-French-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty has been delayed for several years, leaving hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese in Vietnam eagerly awaiting the relief this treaty would provide. The situation is particularly urgent. It is appropriate to cable the Ministry again to examine and approve this matter, and earnestly request that you promptly consult with the French Minister to conclude the treaty as soon as possible to reassure the overseas Chinese. This is our most sincere plea.

Respectfully,

Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce of the Republic of China (Stamped)"

The Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Southern Vietnam and the Overseas Chinese Association for Promoting the Sino-French Commercial Treaty have also submitted a document to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and sent a copy to the National Federation of Commerce for reference. The original text is as follows: "We respectfully submit this document regarding the revision of the Sino-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty and request the establishment of preferential tariffs for Chinese goods imported into Vietnam. On September 24th, we received a reply dated September 12th, No. Ou 8143, stating: 'We have received your submission. Upon investigation, the Sino-French-Vietnamese Treaty of May 16, 1930, clearly stipulates the rights that overseas Chinese should enjoy in terms of personal safety and commerce. Once the appendixes A and B are signed and the new treaty is implemented, the various unfavorable treatments currently suffered by overseas Chinese can be gradually improved. This Ministry will naturally negotiate strongly with the French side based on the interests of overseas Chinese to ensure the implementation of the new treaty. Please inform us accordingly.' We immediately announced this to the overseas Chinese in Vietnam for their information. On September 20th, we sent a submission reporting the Vietnamese government's plan to force Chinese merchants to use Western bookkeeping methods, and attached a French regulation regarding this matter. We trust that it has already reached your esteemed attention. We are now attaching a list of the types of Chinese goods imported into Vietnam and their new and old tariff rates for your consideration. We also request that you negotiate with the French government to reduce tariffs on Chinese goods entering Vietnam. For goods that previously enjoyed special preferential tariff rates, we request that they be restored. For other Chinese goods, we request that they receive the most favored nation tariff rate, so that Chinese goods can regain their sales channels in Vietnam and save the industry and commerce of hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese in Vietnam. Furthermore, we are extremely concerned and eager to know the progress of the discussions between your ministry and the representatives of the French government regarding the Sino-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty. The industry and commerce of overseas Chinese are in a desperate situation. The only hope lies in the implementation of the Sino-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty, reducing tariffs on Chinese goods, and improving the treatment of overseas Chinese. Therefore, they are struggling to survive, awaiting a change in the situation. We implore your Ministry to save them and to inform us of the progress of the Sino-Vietnamese Commercial Treaty negotiations to appease public opinion. This would be a great kindness."

Shanghai Organizations Held a Grand Welcome Meeting for Hu Wenhu Yesterday 117

Attended by Over Four Thousand People, a Great Success

Newspaper Association Held a Luncheon Banquet

Overseas Chinese magnate Hu Wenhu has been warmly welcomed by all sectors since his arrival in Shanghai. He has been visiting the city center and major factories for several days. Yesterday at noon, the Shanghai Newspaper Association held a banquet for Mr. Hu Wenhu at the Tongxinglou Restaurant. At 3 PM, Shanghai organizations held the Shanghai Organizations Welcome Mr. Hu Wenhu Meeting at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge. Over four thousand representatives attended. Mr. Hu arrived on time, entering the venue amidst the melodious military music and enthusiastic applause from the representatives. After Mr. Hu arrived, he announced the opening of the meeting. The meeting was very enthusiastic. The details are recorded below:

Newspaper Association Banquet 118

The Shanghai Newspaper Association, including Ma Yinliang, Wang Boqi, Huang Bohui, Xiong Shaohao, Pan Gongzhan, Guan Ji'an, Wu Shirong, etc., held a luncheon banquet for the leader of the Nanyang overseas Chinese, Mr. Hu Wenhu, at the Tongxinglou Hall yesterday at 12 noon. They also invited Hu Zhongying, Ye Guisong, Li Dachao, Hu Guigeng, Lang Jingshan, etc. to accompany him. Over thirty guests and hosts attended. During the banquet, Chairman Yuan Yeyu delivered a welcome speech, stating: "Today, I especially represent the colleagues of our association to welcome Mr. Hu. Mr. Hu is visiting for the second time since his return to China in 1929. We have a deep impression of Mr. Hu. Today, I would like to mention a few points to show our admiration: (1) Mr. Hu has established many newspapers in Nanyang and South China. The Sing Tao Daily in Singapore has become the center of public opinion in Nanyang. Therefore, Mr. Hu is not only a magnate businessman but also a great supporter of the newspaper industry. (2) Only an entire country can fight with other countries, but Mr. Hu can fight the world alone. This is truly commendable. (3) Mr. Hu repeatedly returns to China, allowing domestic compatriots to communicate news and connect feelings with overseas Chinese. Mr. Hu is a powerful facilitator. (4) Mr. Hu has established many businesses abroad, especially those that promote Chinese culture, which has contributed to the country. All of the above are the reasons why we welcome Mr. Hu today. I would like to raise a glass to wish Mr. Hu good health." Then, Mr. Hu Guigeng delivered a reply speech on behalf of Mr. Hu, stating: "I am honored to be able to meet with the leaders of the press today. Mr. Hu is a layman in the newspaper industry. I am grateful for this opportunity to learn from you. As for the four points mentioned by the chairman, they are an overstatement of Mr. Hu. I am truly unworthy. However, I will work harder with everyone's guidance, and I hope that you will provide more guidance to overseas Chinese so that they can pay attention to investing in the motherland and supporting construction." The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves and did not disperse until 2:30 PM.

Welcome Meeting by All Sectors 119

Attending Representatives: The representatives of various agencies and organizations who attended the welcome meeting for Mr. Hu Wenhu yesterday included Luo Zhiqing from the Sichuan Provincial Government, Hu Shuyi from the Shanghai Children's Welfare Association, Jiang Wenyu from the China Vocational Education Society, Lin Zhongke from Pudong Middle School, Wu Zhihao from the China National Products Production and Sales Association, Zhu Shaoping from the Global Student Association, Pan Gongzhan from the Chen Bao Newspaper, Lin Meiyan from the Dagong Vocational School, Cheng Shouchong from the Shanghai Machine Association, Cao Yunxiang from the Industrial and Commercial Management Association, Fan Hansheng, Consul General to Korea, Lin Kanghou from the National Federation of Commerce, Guan Jiongzhi from the Local Association, Mu Ouchu, Chu Huiseng from the Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association, and over four thousand others.

A Glimpse of the Venue: The venue was originally scheduled to be at the New Asia Restaurant, but due to the large number of participating organizations, it was temporarily moved to the City Chamber of Commerce. At the entrance of the City Chamber of Commerce, the Party and national flags were hung, as well as a bamboo cloth banner that read "Shanghai Organizations Welcome Mr. Hu Wenhu Meeting." Boy Scouts were stationed inside to maintain order. Lianhua Film Company also sent cameramen to the venue to film the meeting. In addition to the Party and national flags and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the rostrum also had framed mirrors sent by Minsheng Middle School, etc., hanging on both sides. A military band was hired to play music at the venue.

Meeting Proceedings: (1) Opening of the meeting; (2) Playing music; (3) All stand at attention; (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party and national flags and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (5) The chairman respectfully reads Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will; (6) The chairman delivers a welcome speech; (7) Speeches; (8) Mr. Hu Wenhu's speech; (9) Playing music; (10) Photography; (11) Adjournment. The presidium consisted of Zhang Shouyong (China Economic Credit Cooperative), Yu Zuoting (Shanghai Chamber of Commerce), Lin Kanghou (National Federation of Commerce), Qiu Hanping (Qiaoguang Middle School), Li Dachao (China Women's Middle School), Liu Daofang (Huahai Vocational Middle School), Wu Yingpei (Overseas Chinese Federation), Wen Lanting (Shanghai Local Association), and Xu Shiying (Drought Relief Association). Chairman Yu Zuoting of the City Chamber of Commerce gave a report first, followed by Zhang Shouyong, Wang Xiaolai, Chu Huiseng, Xu Tongxiong, Qu Wenliu, etc., who delivered speeches in succession. Finally, Hu Wenhu delivered a reply speech, followed by photography and adjournment. It was already after 5 PM.

Chairman's Speech: Yu Zuoting, Chairman of the City Chamber of Commerce, delivered a welcome speech, saying, "Mr. Hu Wenhu has carried on his father's business and has been doing business in Burma for more than seventy years. With his sophisticated talent and unique insights, he has been able to withstand the tides of the world market downturn and the decline of overseas Chinese businesses. His business has grown year by year. Judging from his achievements, among the overseas Chinese in Burma, apart from the late Mr. Lin Zhenzong of Fujian, Mr. Hu is undoubtedly the most prominent. We have admired his demeanor for many years. However, due to the vastness of the sea and sky, it has been difficult to meet him. We have only been able to express our admiration privately for his business. Now, we are fortunate that he has returned to the motherland for inspection. His visit coincides with the 73rd anniversary of his father, Mr. Ziqin, going to Burma. Two generations of hard work have created this great cause, opening up a glorious history for the overseas Chinese in Burma. This is even more meaningful than celebrating an individual's 70th birthday. Our association has prepared some refreshments today to hold this welcome meeting, which is nothing less than a celebration of the success of Mr. Hu and his father's seventy-year career in Burma. We are deeply delighted to have you here. It is often said that the British territories are all over the world, so their national flag has no sunset. Although our country's political power is not as good as theirs, the overseas Chinese are diligent and hardworking. Without the protection of the state, their footprints are all over the five continents. They often start from scratch and succeed. They can then use the capital earned from their hard work to benefit the motherland. Mencius said, 'Those who wait for King Wen to rise are ordinary people. As for heroes, they will rise even without King Wen.' Only our overseas Chinese are capable of this kind of courage. Therefore, our association is holding this welcome meeting today not only to celebrate the success of Mr. Hu's personal career but also to represent the Chinese people in expressing our gratitude to Mr. Hu for his continued support of the motherland's cause. On the one hand, we want to take this opportunity to show that the motherland is intensifying its construction, and it is in great need of the enthusiastic support of overseas Chinese. Our association knows that most overseas Chinese are struggling in adversity, and we have not heard that the Chinese people have provided any real protection. It is truly shameful to give without receiving. However, the protection of overseas Chinese and the prosperity of the motherland are closely related. To prosper the motherland, we must start by intensifying construction. Mr. Hu has a clear understanding of the situation, so he has repeatedly invested heavily in the motherland's construction, never tiring. This spirit of public service is the key to the revival of our nation and can serve as an example for the general public in the country. We believe that there will be those who will rise up in response to this trend. As the saying goes, words are limited, but the meaning is endless. Today, distinguished guests have arrived, and time is precious. I dare not bore you with lengthy words. I will just briefly state my thoughts and hope for your correction."

Speeches from All Sectors: After Yu's speech, Zhang Shouyong spoke, saying, "Today, Shanghai organizations welcome Mr. Hu Wenhu because he has made great contributions to society and because he is overseas but does not forget his motherland. Mr. Hu has inherited his father's business, worked hard, and gradually expanded it. His purpose in developing his business is to help the development of all social undertakings, such as education, journalism, and charity. Those who have received Mr. Hu's help are everywhere. Today, the country is suffering from natural and man-made disasters, which have plunged the people into deep water and fire. We hope that Mr. Hu can maintain his past spirit and continue to take effective measures to save us from this crisis. At a time when the country is making every effort to promote industry and commerce, we also expect Mr. Hu to do his best to invest." Wang Xiaolai spoke, saying, "Mr. Hu is an overseas Chinese who does not forget his motherland. Mr. Hu is an overseas Chinese who promotes the sale of national products abroad. Mr. Hu is an overseas Chinese who promotes industry. Mr. Hu can show his great personality everywhere. Therefore, Shanghai organizations have given him such a warm welcome." Chu Huiseng spoke, saying, "Today, there are disaster victims everywhere in the country. Taking Zhejiang as an example, millions of people have been affected by the drought. Mr. Hu has a heart to save the world, and he will surely do his best to help these disaster-stricken compatriots." Xu Tongxiong spoke, saying, "We hope that Mr. Hu can return to the country this time to conduct a detailed inspection, and we especially hope that Mr. Hu can travel to the Northwest. The Northwest is a treasure trove of our country. We hope that Mr. Hu can use his spirit of investing in industry to help the government develop the Northwest." Finally, Qu Wenliu spoke, saying, "Everyone knows Mr. Hu's spirit of loving his motherland. There is no need to say more. At a time when the country is in trouble, Mr. Hu will surely provide great help to his motherland."

Mr. Hu's Reply: After the representatives finished their speeches, Hu Wenhu stood up and gave a speech, saying, "This time I returned to China to visit the new Shanghai plan and inspect the new construction in various places. I have been warmly welcomed by all sectors since arriving in Shanghai, and I feel honored and ashamed. I am even more embarrassed that the newspapers have mistakenly praised me as a great entrepreneur and a great philanthropist. It is the duty of all mankind to use surplus wealth to seek the welfare of the society and the people. I inherited my father's ambition and managed the pharmaceutical business. Although I have accumulated a lot of savings over the decades, I have always regarded it as something external. Money is both omnipotent and evil. If it is used well, it will certainly benefit the people. If it is not used well, it will not only create sins for oneself but also harm future generations. Although I do not hate evil capitalists, I often feel afraid of being a capitalist. Therefore, I am willing to use all the profits from my business every year for charitable and public welfare purposes, rather than buying land and houses and boasting about my wealth. The shops of our various branches are all rented from others, which is proof of this. However, these actions are only to fulfill my wishes and do what I can. People in the society have added the title of philanthropist to me. Although your intention is to promote good, it is very good, but I feel that the name is more than the reality, and I can't help but feel ashamed. In the future, I will work harder and do my best to serve the society. I plan to set up a hospital in each province of our country in five or ten years to repay the kindness of you and the people in society. If the rich can use their surplus money to seek the welfare of the society and the people, then use the wealth of the society to do the things of the society. Those who get it from the society should use it in the society. There is no class, and there is no struggle. This is my personal belief. Today, I am honored to receive your love, and I will mention it. As for visiting the city center and the new construction in various places in the past few days, I feel very satisfied. In particular, the Greater Shanghai plan is admirable. Eight years ago, I came to Shanghai and visited Jiangwan, Wusong, and other places. At that time, I felt that the land there was very good, but it was like wasteland, which was a pity. I had a vision of Greater Shanghai in my heart. Unexpectedly, when I revisit this place today, the Greater Shanghai in my dream has been gradually realized. How happy is it! Today, I am grateful to the organizations for holding a meeting to welcome me. There are many things I want to talk to you about, but due to time constraints, I can only briefly mention one or two. I will listen to your teachings again when I have the opportunity. Now, I would like to thank you very sincerely."
