Five Banks Continued to Discuss the Wei River Diversion Loan Contract Yesterday 124

An Agreement Can Be Reached After One or Two More Meetings

The Loan Disbursement Method Has Been Determined, and Funds Will Be Allocated at Any Time

According to Xin Xin News Agency, after Lei Baohua, Director of the Shaanxi Provincial Construction Department, consulted with the borrowing banks at the Central Bank the day before yesterday, the Wei River Diversion Loan in Shaanxi Province has been determined to be 1.5 million yuan, with the water and land tax of the Luo, Jing, and Wei canals as the guarantee fund, and it is stipulated that the loan will be repaid within three years. It is learned that the borrowing banks continued to meet at the Central Bank on the third floor yesterday afternoon at 4 PM to discuss the loan contract. Chen Xing and Zhou Bangxin from the Central Bank, Zhang Peishen and Jin Guobao from the Bank of Communications, Liu Yingnong and Cheng Muhao from the Bank of China, Zou Bingwen from the Shanghai Bank, and Chen Liting from the Jincheng Bank, etc., attended. The meeting did not end until after 5 PM. After the meeting, Zhou Bangxin, Deputy Manager of the Central Bank, told a reporter from Xin Xin News Agency that the 1.5 million yuan Wei River Diversion Loan was borrowed by five banks: Central, China, Communications, Shanghai, and Jincheng. It is inaccurate to say that it was borrowed by six banks. Today's meeting continued to discuss some details in the contract and the distribution of the loan amount among the five banks. There are no major problems, and an agreement can be reached and signed after one or two more meetings. As for the loan disbursement method, it has been decided that funds will be allocated at any time. The annual interest rate is still being discussed.

Various Banks Have Fully Deposited Savings Guarantees 125

Equivalent to Over 70 Million Silver Yuan

The Savings Guarantee Reserve Custody Committee of Banks has already completed its review of the securities of the quarter guarantee of savings of various banks, and they have been handed over to the Central Bank. A portion of the insurance treasury has been opened separately for safekeeping. The total amount of the guarantee is equivalent to approximately 70 million silver yuan. Except for the Universal Savings Society, all other banks have fully deposited. The Ministry of Finance will handle the negotiations with the Savings Society upon its request.

Sea Yuan Steamer Completes Factory Inspection Today, Reception Ceremony to be Held Tomorrow 126

Minister Zhu Comes to Shanghai to Attend

The China Merchants Bureau's new steamer, the Hai Yuan, has undergone continuous inspections since entering the Jiangnan Shipyard and is nearing completion. It is expected to leave the factory today and dock at the Jinliyuan Wharf. The reception ceremony will be held tomorrow. The details are as follows:

Completion of Inspection and Departure from Factory: According to the contract, the ship was to be delivered in Shanghai, so it entered the Jiangnan Shipyard for a detailed inspection of all parts. The inspection costs were borne by the Swan Hunter Shipbuilders, who built the ship. The inspection has been ongoing for eight days since the ship entered the factory. Shen Jiyun, the general shipmaster of the China Merchants Bureau, has also been inspecting the ship daily and listening to inspection reports. The ship is expected to complete inspection and leave the factory today, moving to Jinliyuan Wharf.

Handover Procedures: The handover procedure involves the Jiangnan Shipyard sending the inspection report to the China Merchants Bureau. Once the bureau deems all parts qualified and in accordance with the contract, a telegram will be sent to London, instructing the supervising committee in the UK to pay the final installment of the ship's price to the shipyard. The shipyard will then telegram its Shanghai representative, Malcolm, to hand over the Hai Yuan to the bureau. Of the eight officers and sixteen sailors sent by the shipyard, all but one engineer will leave the ship, and the officers and sailors assigned by the bureau will board the ship to take up their duties. As of yesterday, the return telegram from the UK had not arrived, so the ship has not yet been handed over.

Reception Ceremony: The bureau will hold a grand ceremony for the reception of the Hai Yuan. It has been scheduled for 2:30 PM tomorrow. Five hundred invitations have already been sent out, including representatives from the military, government, press, and various sectors of Shanghai, as well as many foreign guests. Minister of Transportation Zhu Jia骅 will represent the bureau as the chairman of the reception ceremony. Director of the Maritime Administration Gao Tingzi will also come to Shanghai to participate in the grand ceremony. (The order of ceremony was published in this newspaper on the 12th of last month)

Crew Boarding: The entire crew has been appointed by the bureau. After the ship arrives at the wharf today, twenty-five service personnel will be the first to board the ship. Personnel in charge of the deck will also be dispatched to board the ship to inspect and receive items on board. The captain and other officers will board the ship and officially assume their duties once the handover telegram arrives from the UK.

Another Two Disaster Prevention Drills to be Held in the City 127

Interview with Director Yang Hu of the Security Department

Another Drill on a Snowy and Cold Night

According to the Central News Agency, Director Yang Hu of the Municipal Security Department told the agency that various party, government, and military agencies in the city had conducted disaster prevention drills starting from the 3rd. Military Expert Discusses Air Defense 128

Technology and Equipment: Our Country's Architecture Largely Ignores These Conditions, While Tokyo, Japan, Has Already Made Preparations

According to the Central News Agency, with the progress of science, the past planar warfare has been transformed into three-dimensional warfare. In addition to actively expanding their air forces, countries are also paying attention to air defense technology and equipment. A Central News Agency reporter met with a military expert who recently returned from overseas inspections. The expert stated that our country's architecture largely ignores air defense conditions and urgently needs to be improved to respond to emergencies. The details of the conversation are recorded below:

Uniformity in Height is Essential: According to the expert, the biggest shortcoming of our country's architecture is the extreme difference in height. Taking Shanghai's buildings as an example, the lower ones, apart from a few bungalows, are mostly two to three stories or even five to six stories, while the higher ones are over ten stories or even twenty stories. The difference in height is extreme, making them easy targets for aerial bombardment. The extreme difference in height makes them easily identifiable from the air, making it easy to determine which ones to bomb. After the great earthquake, all the buildings in Tokyo had similar heights. When Tokyo held air defense drills, it was discovered that the building of Tokyo's largest department store was higher than other buildings. The department store was notified to demolish one floor to eliminate the target for bombing. This is the responsibility of the government. Our country's recent palace-style buildings are often painted in conspicuous red and green colors, which also makes them easy targets for bombing and goes against air defense conditions.

Underground Facilities are Necessary: Recently, the top floors of new-style buildings in various countries around the world have flat terraces for deploying large nets and stacking sandbags to prevent bomb explosions during air raids. Underground facilities are also necessary for storing important documents and serving as shelters in case of emergency. In contrast, our country's architecture focuses on aesthetics and is not practical at all. This is deeply unsettling. This is the responsibility of architects, and it is hoped that they will pay attention to it.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Executive and Supervisory Committee Meeting Discusses Commercial Registration Law 129

Resolution to Support Article 9 of the Draft Law

Request to Supplement Article 2 of the Draft Law

According to the New Voice News Agency, since Article 681 of the Civil Code's Law of Obligations stipulates that partners are jointly liable for partnership debts, the business community across the country has requested amendments due to conflicts with legislative fairness, policies, and the economic status quo of our country. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce also submitted two petitions to the Legislative Yuan in March and June of last year, requesting amendments. The Legislative Yuan decided to draft a Commercial Registration Law to remedy this. The draft law has now been completed by the Legislative Yuan, reviewed in meetings, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has been requested to send representatives Chen Zheqing and Luo Qinghua to Beijing to express their opinions. The research was very detailed. The two representatives have now returned to Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees to discuss the matter. Yu Zuoting, Jin Runxiang, Chen Zheqing, Ke Ganchen, Ma Shaoquan, Zheng Chengqing, Chen Yizhou, Hu Xiyuan, Zheng Zenan, Pan Xusheng, Ma Jiliang, Cheng Yujie, Luo Qinghua, Fang Jiaobo, and others attended. Yu Zuoting chaired the meeting. After the formalities, Chen Zheqing and Luo Qinghua reported on their experience attending the meeting in Beijing. Then, the draft Commercial Registration Law was discussed. It was resolved that Article 9 of the draft, which stipulates that "If the names and addresses of the partners and the types and amounts of their contributions have been registered by the individuals with the competent authority in the location of the business, they shall be liable for sharing losses within the limit of their contributions. The same shall apply when shares are transferred or changed," was unanimously supported, and it was hoped that it would be passed smoothly. Regarding Article 2 of the draft, which states that "Commercial registration shall be made by the parties concerned with the competent authority in the location of the business," it was requested to be supplemented to state that those with trade associations should have the association forward it to the Chamber of Commerce, and those without trade associations should have the Chamber of Commerce directly forward it, in order to comply with Article 7 of the Legislative Yuan's amended Trade Association Law, which states that trade companies and firms should join the association, etc.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Submits Petition Urging Amendment of New Stamp Tax Law 130

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce submitted a further petition to the Executive Yuan urging the amendment of the new Stamp Tax Law, stating that: This petition concerns the urgent matter of requesting the amendment of the Stamp Tax Law. On the 7th of this month, we received a letter from the Silk and Satin Trade Association, stating that they had received a joint letter from 175 member companies, stating that after reading the newspaper reports, they were shocked to learn that the draft Stamp Tax Law prepared by the Legislative Yuan stipulates that the tax rates for invoices, bills, receipts, etc., are one cent for amounts from three yuan to ten yuan, and an additional one cent for every additional ten yuan. The stamp tax for stocks, loan agreements, contracts, etc., is two cents per hundred yuan, and the stamp tax for books is two jiao per year, which is several times or even dozens of times higher than the provisional regulations. They were extremely alarmed by this. They stated that in recent years, economic recession has spread across the country, and silk merchants are suffering from high tax rates and sluggish business conditions, making it difficult to maintain their businesses. They are unable to cope with the increased stamp tax rates, and the progressive calculation method is particularly burdensome. They requested the Chamber of Commerce to forward their request to the government, urging the government to consider the difficulties of merchants and reduce the tax rates to alleviate their plight, etc. (omitted). Based on this, we request that your association quickly forward our request, urging the government to consider the difficulties of merchants and appropriately reduce the stamp tax rates and abolish the progressive calculation method to maintain commerce. This will be greatly appreciated. We have already telegraphed the Central Political Council directly on October 13, requesting that it correct the situation based on the principles of the Stamp Tax Law formulated last year. We also submitted another petition to your council on October 18, requesting that you forward it to the National Government to temporarily not announce the implementation of the law until the Central Political Council has corrected it. Two weeks have passed since then, and we have not received a reply. We have repeatedly received detailed information from the paper, tea, and timber industries, requesting us to continue to appeal. Now, we have received a letter from the association with the same request. The amendment of the tax law is truly the universal and urgent wish of merchants. We hereby submit another written petition for your review and approval, urging you to investigate and approve the various points mentioned in the previous petitions as soon as possible, as it will be in the public interest.

China Foreign Famine Relief Committee Conducting Emergency Relief in Various Regions 134

Haining and Haiyan: The China Foreign Famine Relief Committee is working hard to raise relief funds due to the severe drought in Haining and Haiyan, but fundraising is difficult. It has jointly launched a campaign with the Jisheng Association and Haining gentry in Shanghai. The Haining gentry raised 20,000 yuan, and the Jisheng Association and the committee jointly contributed 20,000 yuan, totaling 40,000 yuan. This is only enough to cover the third and fifth districts of Haining. The investigation was initiated, and although the investigation of the fifth district has been completed, there are 10,780 households in need of relief. Most households have four to five to seven to eight people. The third district is still under investigation, but it is also a significant number. Currently, there are too few resources for too many people, making it difficult to distribute them. It is reported that the three organizations will each raise another 5,000 yuan, totaling 15,000 yuan, bringing the total to 55,000 yuan. It is still unknown how this will be handled. The committee has also decided to allocate 5,000 yuan to Haiyan and will soon begin distributing emergency relief.

Liyang and Yixing: The disaster situation in these two areas is the most tragic and severe in Jiangsu Province. The China Foreign Famine Relief Committee has decided to allocate 10,000 yuan for emergency relief. The Wuxi Red Swastika Society has also raised 25,000 yuan for relief and is jointly conducting relief efforts. Because there are too many disaster victims in the area and too little relief money, there are concerns that riots will occur. The Red Swastika Society has raised another 10,000 yuan, and the China Foreign Famine Relief Committee has raised another 5,000 yuan. Shanghai gentry, recognizing the severity and scope of the disaster, have also contributed 4,000 to 5,000 yuan. They are jointly purchasing flour, and Lu Bohong will go to preside over the relief distribution. The China Foreign Famine Relief Committee has also raised 5,000 yuan for emergency relief in Yixing and will proceed with it in order.

Jiangbei and Jiangpu: The drought in Jiangbei is extremely severe, especially in Jiangpu. It is reported that the committee has allocated more than 8,000 yuan and is cooperating with cooperatives to distribute seeds and provide emergency relief.

Launching Ceremony Today

The Da Zhonghua Machinery Shipyard, located on Junpu Road, Yangshupu, is founded by Yang Junsheng, a renowned Chinese shipbuilder. The shipyard has been established for more than ten years, has extensive experience, and has achieved excellent results, which has long been praised by the shipping and mechanical engineering industries. This time, it won a bid of more than 400,000 yuan to build a new ship for the Dada Steamer Company. The ship is 238 feet long, 38 feet wide, has a draft of 10 feet 6 inches, and a displacement of more than 1,800 tons. It can carry 1,200 tons. It is the largest steamer built by a Chinese shipyard. Other features, such as increased speed, fuel savings, and fire protection equipment, are unique to Chinese steamers. The ship has been under construction for many days, and the hull has now been completed. The launching ceremony will be held at the factory at 2:00 PM on the 9th of this month. Construction Took Four Years and Cost 3.5 Million Yuan

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency obtained the following details from the Four Banks yesterday:

Domestic Materials: The new building of the Four Banks Savings Society on Jing'an Temple Road is 22 stories high. Fire on Tangqiao Road, Pudong, Lasts for Two Hours 139

No Water Nearby to Put Out the Fire

Three Houses Completely Destroyed

Three bungalows were built on the open space at the south end of Sangguan Hall, Tangqiao Road, Pudong. The He Xinglong incense shop was opened there. The owner is a woman surnamed Jiang from Tongzhou, who employed more than a dozen workers. Yesterday evening around 8:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out for unknown reasons. The workers were unable to put it out, and it quickly spread. The nearby police officers sounded the whistle for help. Because there was no hydrant nearby, dozens of villagers could only draw water to put out the fire, which was to no avail. After burning for about two hours, all three houses were completely destroyed. Huang, the chief of the Tangqiao Police Station, ordered the fire victim Jiang to be summoned to the station for questioning.

Night Soil Worker Smilingly Pats Woman's Shoulder, Woman Hangs Herself in Tears 140

Husband Misunderstands and Thinks It's a Joke

Tragedy Starts with a Trivial Matter, One Life Lost

Chen Yanghe, a 42-year-old man from Yancheng, and his wife Chen Fu, a 45-year-old woman, had two daughters and four sons. The sons are named Huaidong, Huainan, Huaixi, and Huaibei. The two daughters had already died. The family of six came to Shanghai to make a living because the rural family in their hometown had gone bankrupt and it was difficult to make a living. They lived at No. 28 Heming Lane, Dakang Lane, Kanti Road, French Concession. Chen set up a private school to teach at No. 26 next door. The four sons were all peddlers, making a living on their own. Chen's wife worked at home. At around 2:00 PM on the 6th of this month, a night soil worker came to collect the monthly fee of two jiao. Fu replied that she had no money and promised to pay it the next day. The night soil worker agreed, smiling and patting Fu on the shoulder several times before leaving. Chen Yanghe happened to see this and blamed his wife for joking with the night soil worker. Feeling wronged and unable to express her anger, she had a sudden thought. At around 10:00 AM the next morning, while her husband was out teaching and the four sons were out working, she committed suicide by hanging herself on the mezzanine on the second floor of the house. Around noon, Chen Yanghe returned home for lunch and discovered it. She had already died of suffocation, and her body was as cold as ice. He reported it to the French Police Department, who sent detectives to investigate the cause of death. Then, the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall Morgue. Yesterday morning, the Second Special Court commissioned Prosecutor Wang Ren and a forensic doctor to examine the body and confirm that Chen Fu had indeed died of hanging herself before death. The body was handed over to her husband, Chen Yanghe, to claim the body and prepare for the funeral.

The Tragic Death of a Child Laborer Examined 141

Ji Qingyuan, a fifteen-year-old from Haimen, was working as a young laborer at the Puyi No. 2 Cotton Mill at No. 8 Labour Sheng Road. At precisely 7:00 PM the night before, while he was working in the factory, a belt on a machine suddenly came loose from its axle. He intended to climb up and put the belt back in place, but unfortunately, the machine was still running. Ji was not careful enough at the time, and his sleeve got caught in the machine. Soon, various parts of his body were also severely crushed. Another worker, Jiang Guisheng, caught sight of the situation and quickly tried to rescue him, but it was too late. The factory took him to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He soon died. The hospital reported to the Putuo Road Police Station in charge of the area, and they ordered detectives to investigate. The body was then taken to Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Local Court appointed Prosecutor Tang, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan, court clerk Wang Zuyi, and others to examine the body. Witness Jiang Guisheng testified that he was thirty-four years old, from Chongming, and a worker at the Puyi Factory. He said that he managed the machine and that the deceased happened to be sweeping the floor next to the machine when he saw the belt come off. Ji then volunteered to go up and install it, but he was not careful enough and was suddenly crushed by the machine. After seeing this, he immediately closed the machine door and tried to save him, but it was already too late, and so on. Ji Wanqing, the deceased's father, also gave a statement. Prosecutor Tang then declared that the deceased, Ji Qingyuan, was indeed injured by a machine and died. The body was handed over to his father, Ji Wanqing, who signed a receipt to take it back for burial.

Continued Hearing of Liang Tongfang's Bombing Case 142

Liang claims his intention was only to warn, not to kill.

The judge argues that kind words and advice should be used instead of throwing bombs.

—Because the case still requires investigation, the hearing is postponed to Saturday.—

Liang Tongfang, a patriotic young man from Shaoxing, was upset about the sale of inferior goods at the Yuelai Southern Goods Store at No. 354 Guangdong Road. So, at noon on the 19th of last month, he carried a bomb with the intention of giving a warning. Unexpectedly, the bomb exploded before he could throw it, injuring four people, including Yuelai staff member Pan Honghe, and seriously injuring Liang himself. He was arrested and taken to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Details have already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide presided over a continued hearing in the Criminal Division. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that since the adjournment, he had repeatedly inquired with Liang about the true situation, but Liang refused to tell the truth. Chinese and foreign detectives from the police station searched Liang's residence at the East Asia Institute of Physical Education and found many leaflets. They contained phrases like "If you do not awaken, you will be annihilated," implying an intention to kill. The defendant previously stated that the bomb would explode one or two minutes after being thrown, but according to the foreign detective chief, this is not true. He brought an identical bomb to court today to prove that it could explode immediately. The Municipal Council is prosecuting under Article 284, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law for attempted murder. Then, the foreign detective chief submitted a report on the use of the bomb. When questioned, Liang Tongfang testified that he went to Yuelai only to give a warning. He first told the store staff to leave and then removed the safety pin from the bomb, but it unexpectedly exploded immediately. If he had not told them to leave, he would not have been so badly injured himself. On the 18th, he and several comrades met at the Heming Hotel. He could not remember the room number but knew that the room was booked under the name of Hong En. The bombs they brought should have exploded one or two minutes after being thrown, but this time it exploded before it was thrown. The leaflets that were seized were delivered by comrades the night after September 18th. On September 18th, he distributed them to various stores, giving them one month to stop buying inferior goods or face annihilation, which was also intended as a warning and not intended to kill. He obtained the bomb after retiring from the Beiping Anti-Traitor Corps. The court then told him that since the government had not ordered a ban on the sale of inferior goods, one should simply advise unscrupulous merchants kindly. (Liang replied:) "Because inferior goods sell well in our country, causing economic panic, no one has ever listened to warnings." The court then asked the foreign detective chief whether Liang Tongfang's claim that the bomb could not kill people was true. (The detective chief replied:) "It can indeed kill many people." Next, Pan Honghe, a staff member of Yuelai Store, testified that he was just finishing his meal and going to work in the store when he saw Liang speaking eloquently. His two colleagues, Fu Rongsheng and Ding Yanzhi, did not understand what he was saying. Liang looked very agitated. He was about to go forward to inquire when the bomb exploded. He was injured in the face and did not know anything else. Police lawyer Wang then stated that the Yuelai Southern Goods Store received a letter on the 5th of this month from an assassination group with its name on it, with two points worth noting: (1) it mentioned using a handgun; (2) it demanded that Yuelai pay 20,000 yuan. He then presented the letter to the court. The court showed the letter to Liang and asked if it was written by his comrades. After reading it, Liang replied that the letter was not written by his comrades but by speculators who were taking advantage of the situation to sabotage their work and profit from it. At this point, the court, finding that further investigation was required, adjourned the hearing to Saturday of this week.

Criminals and loot handed over together

Joint Meeting of Various Organizations Decides to Bury Pan Hongsheng in the May 30th Cemetery 148

Also passes a resolution to erect a memorial to Martyr Pan

Concession authorities refuse to issue a funeral permit

The Shanghai All Circles Assistance to Patriotic Martyrs Committee convened a joint meeting of representatives from various organizations at the committee's location at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss and decide on matters such as public burial and the erection of a monument. In addition, the British and French Concession police authorities have refused to issue permits for Martyr Pan's funeral on the 11th, which has caused great indignation among all circles. It has been decided to continue negotiations. The details learned by the reporter of the Xin Xin News Agency are as follows:

Representatives' Meeting Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, various organizations convened a joint meeting at the City General Chamber of Commerce. Over one hundred people attended, including Chen Jiufeng, Chen Binghui, Wang Jingdong, Qu Zhenhua, Zhang Xianfang, etc. Chen Jiufeng, Chen Peide, and Liu Zhongying served as the presidium. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Burial location: (Resolution) It was decided to designate the May 30th Cemetery as the burial place for Martyr Pan and to send a letter to the board of directors of the May 30th Cemetery to be handled by the funeral committee. (2) Erecting a monument to commemorate Martyr Pan Hongsheng: (Resolution) Passed. (3) Compensation: (Resolution) To submit a request to the government for compensation and to seek donations from all circles to compensate the family. The method will be formulated by the Patriotic Martyrs Association. (4) Date of memorial service: (Resolution) Set for December 7th. (5-7) To be handled by the funeral committee. (5) Present a request to the Fifth National Congress to prohibit the police from abusing electric shocks: (Resolution) Passed. (6) To publish a declaration against the illegal sentencing by the concession authorities, Tao Leqin was appointed to draft it. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Refusal to Issue Permit Representatives from various organizations, Qu Zhenhua and Zhang Xianfang, reported on the progress of applying for permits from the British and French authorities. The representatives reported that they applied to the British and French Concession police departments for funeral permits today but were refused. All requests were rejected. When repeatedly asked for the reason for the refusal, the reason given was that Pan Hongsheng's actions had political implications and that there was a fear that gangsters would take the opportunity to cause trouble along the way. After the representatives explained in detail and reduced the number of people attending the funeral, the authorities still insisted on not issuing the permit. The representatives asked for instructions from all the representatives.

Expressions from All Circles Upon learning of the above situation, representatives from all circles were indignant. They all believed that Martyr Pan sacrificed himself for the patriotic movement, which was very obvious. How could it be that the citizens of our country are not allowed to pass through the concessions leased to foreigners because they are patriotic? How can we accept the obstruction of the patriotic national movement of our citizens? Even if it is said that Pan Hongsheng's actions did contain undesirable political motives, he is already dead. Why should he not be allowed to be buried? If there is a fear that unscrupulous elements will take the opportunity to cause trouble, then the police have the responsibility to maintain law and order. According to the representatives' report, the authorities said that they could take a detour through the Chinese territory. However, the Xijin Guild Hall is located on Haining Road in the Public Concession. How will that be handled? Fortunately, Pan lived in the Chinese territory. If he lived in the concession, the coffin would not be able to leave. It is not known whether the authorities have regulations for refusing to issue funeral permits. Since the concession authorities said that there was no basis for it, the representatives' meeting should send representatives to continue to fight for it. Otherwise, the concession authorities will be responsible for any disputes.

Public Memorial by Righteous Army Members of the Shanghai Citizens' Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army held a meeting at the funeral committee of Pan Martyr at 8:00 AM yesterday to discuss donations and public memorial methods. Wu Huanwen, Hong Liehun, Ni Huaixin, Zhong Zhixiang, Xie Yuhai, etc. were present. Wu Huanwen was elected as the chairman, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Please publicly elect the convener: (Resolution) Wu Huanwen, Hong Liehun, Ni Huaixin, Zhong Zhixiang, Xie Yuhai, etc. were publicly elected as the convener. (2) How should we help Pan Martyr, who was poor after his death?: (Resolution) A. Each person should contribute a funeral gift and donate as much as possible. B. Each person should do their best to gather scattered comrades and enthusiastically donate and participate. C. Please ask the funeral committee to include an advertisement to gather comrades to inform everyone. (3) How to participate in the funeral ceremony: (Resolution) Use the Zhifu ritual to show respect. Temporary motion: (1) Please ask the Assistance to Patriotic Martyrs Committee to save waste and give substantial benefits to the family: (Resolution) Send a letter to the Assistance to Patriotic Martyrs Committee to pay attention. (2) The Citizens' Daily and the National Goods Movement Newspaper will publish special editions on the 11th of this month. Please ask comrades to contribute articles enthusiastically: (Resolution) Passed. (3) The public memorial will be held at 2:00 PM on November 10th: (Resolution) Passed. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM.

A Glimpse of Donations Liu Chunshan has been broadcasting on the Huaxing Radio Station for days to encourage donations from all circles. The donors have become more and more enthusiastic. Yesterday, the following donations were received: (1) Xu's laundry old lady, eight jiao; (2) female worker Song Jinmei, three jiao and two fen; (3) elementary school student Qu Zongjun's saved candy money, one yuan; (4) eight-year-old Zhao Yuanyuan, two jiao and eighteen copper coins. All were delivered by Liu Chunshan. The rest of the Ningbo Bank's receipts will be reported later.

Broadcasting Propaganda Wu Zhihao, general manager of the Shanghai National Goods Company across from the Rainbow Temple on Nanjing Road, and manager Lu Qisheng have always held the purpose of saving the country. Therefore, the company sells various daily national goods at low prices to promote sales. It is learned that Wu and Lu deeply regret the passing of Patriot Bo Hongsheng and are especially saddened by the family's cries for food. They invited the famous Shanghai comedian Liu Chunshan and others to broadcast the deeds of Pan Martyr on the Huaxing Radio Station and plead for the family, hoping that all ladies and gentlemen will uphold their patriotic enthusiasm and generously donate to help.

Girl Burned to Death in Fire in Ren Zhi Lane, Wuchang Road 154

It is believed that she was knocked down by the smoke after the fire broke out, leading to this tragedy. The police are still investigating the cause of the fire.

Using Yang Zinan as an Agent to Defraud Funds for Overseas Passports 155

Qingtian People Scammed While Seeking Livelihood

Police Requested to Pursue and Arrest

Xiang Zefei, Chen Fanglin, Wu Meifa, Liu Zhenxing, Chen Yanhan, Zhou Ronglu, and others from Qingtian, Zhejiang Province, faced bankruptcy in their rural areas and lacked means to make a living. They planned to go abroad to do business and reluctantly scraped together 300 to 400 yuan each for travel expenses and passports. They entrusted a fellow townsman, Yang Zinan, to handle the matter. Xiang and the others then came to Shanghai from their hometowns and stayed at the Wu Tongchun Inn on Danfeng Road in the Nanshi district. They agreed with Yang to pay 400 yuan each, promising that they could go abroad within a month after payment. Unexpectedly, Xiang and the others waited in Shanghai for over a month without any news. When they inquired with Yang, Yang claimed that those going to countries like Austria and Germany had to go through Haiwei and enter via Siberia. Xiang and the others were going abroad for the first time and obeyed Yang's instructions, so they dared not offend him. However, after waiting another half month, there was still no news. Living in Shanghai was quite expensive, so they agreed with Yang to temporarily return to their hometowns and come to Shanghai again after the passports were processed. Who knew that after returning home for over a month, there was still no news? They came to Shanghai a few days ago to meet with Yang, but Yang only gave them a Tianjin boat ticket. When they questioned him about the passport, he said to pick it up in Haishenwai. Seeing that Yang's words were evasive and that it was not a Haishenwai boat ticket, Xiang and the others feared being trafficked as coolies. They were about to hand Yang over to the local police station, but Yang was alert and escaped. The six of them presented a list of the defrauded funds to the Yimiao Police Station a few days ago, requesting that they be strictly pursued, arrested, and punished.

Young Girl Shot in the Leg at Pear Blossom Brothel 157

Young Customer Goes to Question Her

Police Search and Arrest the Assailant

At around 11 PM last night, a middle-aged man dressed in fine clothes and wearing glasses went to the Pear Blossom Brothel at No. 8, Lane 1, Fuxiang Li, Guangxi Road, for entertainment. It is said that he was acquainted with Pear Blossom Girl (Zhang Sujuan, 17 years old, from Lujiabang, Kunshan County) in the brothel and had been intimate with her. He had recently heard that the girl had taken another lover, so he went to question her. Unexpectedly, they disagreed, and the customer pulled out a self-defense pistol, firing a shot at the girl's leg before fleeing. After being shot, the girl fell to the ground and cried for help. The patrolling police arrived upon hearing the commotion, but the assailant had already fled. They immediately notified the fire department to send an ambulance to take her to the hospital. As the injury was to her leg, it was not serious. As for the customer's name, it was later learned that it was Chen Xin, who works at the Yifeng Enamel Factory. One theory is that Chen was drunk and playing with the gun, causing the accident. After sending detectives to investigate, the police are searching for the assailant and have reportedly apprehended him.

Verdict in the Zhang Xiangwen et al. Case 158

Ms. Wang, whose given name is Zhifen, wife of Li Shilin, a local resident of No. 24, Shangxianfang, Xiafei Road, French Concession, was in her seventh month of pregnancy on June 29th of this year. Li sent her to the Shangxian Hall Maternity Hospital behind Shangxianfang to await delivery. She gave birth to a son that day. Unexpectedly, three days later, the mother suddenly developed puerperal fever. As the hospital did not treat her, she was immediately taken home, where she died after doctors were called in for treatment but were ineffective. Later, Li Shilin believed that the hospital had been negligent in their duties and hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Second Special Court's Criminal Division, accusing Zhang Xiangwen, the hospital's director, Ge Chenghui, a doctor, and Gu Qin, the head nurse, of negligence in their duties, resulting in death due to negligence, and requesting that they be interrogated and punished according to the law. After receiving the complaint, Judge Wang Gangxu repeatedly held court sessions, summoning both parties for questioning, and requested the Chinese Medical Association to conduct an appraisal. The debate was declared closed, and a date was set for the verdict. The previous reports have chronicled each of these events. Yesterday afternoon was the date set for the verdict in the case. Both parties, accompanied by their lawyers, arrived at the court to await instructions. At 2:45 PM, Judge Wang announced the verdict in the criminal court, stating that Zhang Xiangwen, Ge Chenghui, and Gu Qin were all found not guilty. It is faintly heard that the plaintiff expressed dissatisfaction with the verdict and will file an appeal after receiving the judgment.

Search and Capture of Stray Dogs in Pudong 159

Hundreds Already Caught

Stray dogs are rampant in various cities and towns along the Pudong coast. During the day, they roam the streets, competing for scraps from various households, and at night, they sleep anywhere. When people in uniform pass by, they bark madly. A supervisor from the Municipal Public Security Bureau was surrounded by stray dogs several times while inspecting Pudong at night. These dogs, especially the mange-ridden ones, are extremely foul and smelly. In view of this, the Municipal Health Bureau, for the sake of a permanent solution, hired dozens of workers to bring dog-catching vehicles to various parts of Pudong. Due to their skillful operations, the stray dogs were caught without exception. The results have been excellent in recent days. Combining the catches from various locations, no fewer than several hundred have been caught.

Letter from the French Concession Taxpayers' Association to the French Municipal Council 160

Regarding the Increased Tax on Jushenyee Sauce Garden

The Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the French Municipal Council yesterday, stating: We respectfully inform you that we received a letter from the Fourth District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation, stating that Jushenyee Sauce Garden, a member business located at No. 187 Sapo Sai Road, reported that in addition to operating a sauce business, they also sell Shaoxing wine. They pay property tax in accordance with the regulations of the French Municipal Council and have obtained a business license. They also pay a monthly wine tax of 2.80 yuan. They have been operating for many years without any problems. Unexpectedly, on August 16th of this year, they suddenly received a notice from the French Public Works Bureau tax collector, stating that starting from September, the wine tax should be increased by 4.20 yuan, for a total of 7 yuan, which is shocking. Upon investigation, wine tax is levied in three grades. Our business is an example of the second grade, paying 2.80 yuan per month. The tax amount has never been changed or increased since the business was established. The sale of Shaoxing wine is a side business, and the scope of business is small. In this time of economic recession, all businesses are struggling to survive. Therefore, although our business also sells Shaoxing wine, there is actually no business. It can be proven through on-site investigation. Now, the bureau ignores the difficulties of businesses and suddenly proposes to increase taxes by a large amount, which is really difficult to bear. Therefore, we specifically request your council to uphold justice and negotiate with the French Public Works Bureau to cancel the increased tax in order to maintain business. Based on this, since the business has not expanded or changed the tax amount, how can the tax be increased? In this autumn of economic decline, it is especially not the time to increase taxes. In addition to sending a separate letter to the French Public Works Bureau requesting the cancellation of the increased tax, we hereby forward the situation to your council for assistance, requesting that you promptly forward a letter to the French Public Works Bureau to maintain the original tax in order to maintain business.

Burglary at the Qi Shan Village Residence on Yu Yuan Road, West Shanghai 161

Three Robbers Escape with Plunder

Police Detectives Arrive, Robbers Long Gone

At about 9:10 AM yesterday, three robbers suddenly came to the home of Xiao Yimin at No. 31, Qishan Village, Yuyuan Road, West Shanghai. One was wearing a navy blue suit, a gray woolen coat, and a bowler hat; another was wearing a gray suit; and the third was wearing a long robe. All spoke the local dialect. Each held a pistol. After entering, they immediately closed the front door and confined the family members to one room. Then, they began to rummage through boxes and cabinets, looting calmly. For about two hours, they stole a savings passbook from the Bank of China with 3,000 yuan, a gold ring inlaid with a ruby, a pearl bracelet, a diamond ring, a pearl ear pick, and two gold treasure rings. After obtaining the loot, they escaped calmly. Upon receiving the report, Director Wang of the Caojiadu Branch immediately ordered officers Long and Yang, as well as the chief and deputy leaders of the detective team, Wu Kezhong and Cao Chuqiao, and police detectives to rush to the scene to apprehend the robbers. However, the robbers were long gone. At the same time, the Jing'an Temple Police Station also sent Chinese and foreign detectives to conduct a detailed investigation and reported the case, awaiting the arrest and punishment of the robbers and recovery of the stolen goods.

Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Four Banks Preparation Treasury

No. 253

The Four Banks Preparation Treasury, jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu Banks, is dedicated to the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, the issuance of banknotes requires a 100% reserve, with at least 60% in cash reserve and up to 40% in security reserve. It is announced weekly, inspected by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The following is a transcript of the 253rd announcement of the Shanghai Preparation Treasury on November 3, 1934: Banknotes in circulation: 29,948,873 yuan. Total reserves: 29,948,873 yuan, including cash reserves of 22,851,173 yuan and security reserves of 7,097,700 yuan.

Letter to the Editor 169

Having read your newspaper's report yesterday about the dispute over medical expenses between patient Pan Jintao and our hospital on Pushi Road, we have found that it does not match the facts at the time. According to the hospital records, Mr. Pan suffered from cerebral hemorrhage, i.e., stroke. When it occurred and he fell to the ground, Mr. Pan's wife was not in the store. The group helped him to his feet and waited approximately half an hour, and only then was the hospital called for a consultation. When the director of our hospital arrived in person to diagnose and examine, Pan was already unconscious, had a feeble pulse and barely could feel it, and his breathing was on the verge of ceasing altogether. Our Doctor Gu therefore said that he could not be saved, but the shop attendants repeatedly begged to be saved. Doctor Gu therefore generously administered two Coramine injections, in the hope of saving his life for one out of ten thousand chances, but due to the excessive delay, he could not be saved and died. Coramine is considered a harmless and useful agent by doctors of all countries. The patient's family tried to deny our hospital's consultation fees and medical expenses, listening to the plan of a neighbor, who reported to the police station, saying that the injection administered by our Doctor Gu contained a toxic substance. Subsequently, the police station delivered the empty injection vial to the forensic doctor for inspection. On the previous day, after a detailed inspection by prosecutor Wang Ren and the two forensic doctors Wei and Jiang, they determined that Pan Jintao had died due to acute illness and that Doctor Gu was not at fault. The report stated that after the injection, the patient was still able to shout once, etc., but the hospital found that the contents are nothing more than hearsay and untrue. In the hospital's sincere concern, such that all sides may know the real truth, rumors were spreading, and the name and reputation of our hospital were damaged, this special letter would like to correct this, and we request that you print this as well. Best wishes, Shude Hospital, November 8.

Special Feature

The Work of the China Foreign Famine Relief Committee on Disaster Prevention (Continued) 170

Road Construction: In the years of the Republic of China 11, the Committee had already begun road construction plans. In the 12th year, it built the motor road from Xiangtan to Baoqing in Hunan Province, which was truly the beginning of promoting the national highway movement. The Committee continued to carry out this road construction project. Taking Guizhou Province as an example, there were no smooth highways by the end of the 15th year of the Republic. In the winter of the 16th year, the Committee cooperated with the Guizhou Provincial Government, employing 100,000 workers to build a model motor road of 500 miles, which was convenient for the people. From September of the 20th year of the Republic to March of the 21st year, the Committee undertook the construction of the highway between Xi'an and Lanzhou, with a total length of 480 miles, converting the original main road into a motor road, using 500,000 yuan (of which 200,000 yuan was allocated by the National Economic Council). All seven steep mountain ridges were leveled with explosives and manual labor, so that the two major cities in the Northwest were connected to each other. At the same time, many culverts and bridges were built. The Committee also built roads on Liupan Mountain in Gansu. The top of the mountain is about 9,000 feet above sea level, and the slope of the road built by the Committee is no more than 7%. It used to take 18 days to travel this road, but now it only takes three or four days by car. Since its establishment, the Committee has opened up 1,993 miles of new roads and repaired 1,296 miles of old roads in fourteen provinces.

Irrigation Projects: The Shilu Canal, ten miles west of Beiping in Hebei Province, was the first irrigation project undertaken by the Committee. It was completed in the 17th year of the Republic, with a cost of 134,040 yuan, so that 70,000 acres of semi-dry farmland in Hebei Province could be irrigated by the Yongding River. During the severe drought from the 17th to the 18th years of the Republic, the Committee's Engineering Department engaged in large-scale irrigation work, using 800,000 yuan to allow the water of the Yellow River to irrigate 1.2 million mu of farmland in Sa County, Suiyuan Province. This is the achievement of the Minsheng Canal. Although the canal was not completely successful, the Committee had a complete plan, so the central government paid great attention to it and has already sent personnel to take over the work to complete the unfinished task. The Jinghui Canal, jointly operated by the Committee and the Shaanxi Provincial Government, cost 1.3 million yuan, of which 750,000 yuan was donated by the Committee. The farmland that has been irrigated has been extremely productive, and land prices have increased accordingly. However, there are many projects that need to be developed in Shaanxi, and the provincial government still hopes for the Committee's assistance.

Future Work and Opportunities: (1) The most important thing the Committee is paying attention to today is the Fen River Diversion Project in Shanxi Province. Surveying has been underway for a year and a half, and the field work has been completed. The surveying and printing of reports cost a total of 100,000 yuan, all paid by Shanxi Province. Furthermore, this surveying includes four rivers outside the Fen River. According to the plan of the Committee's Engineering Department, the Fen River alone requires 1.27 billion yuan, of which 800 million yuan is for disaster prevention and 470 million yuan is for dredging. In this way, even in the event of severe drought, there is no fear of lack of water, and annual production can be increased. If this plan can be implemented, Shanxi Province will see countless benefits, and the livelihoods of 20 million people can be improved.

(2) In the lower reaches of the Yellow River between Shaanxi and Shanxi provinces, hydropower can be used for grinding and electricity generation to develop industries. The Committee is currently studying and designing this, and the report will be published this autumn.

(3) Developing the Hetao area west of Baotou requires a surveying fee of 40,000 yuan. If this plan can be implemented, 6 million mu of farmland can be irrigated, and the benefits will be endless.

(4) There are many other river courses whose situations are not yet known, and they all have great value for urgent research, in order to start construction as soon as possible for the benefit of the people. (End)

Sports News

The Opening of the Third Shanghai Middle School Joint Sports Meet Causes a Sensation in Xujiahui 171

The audience reached over 15,000 people

Two records broken in yesterday's four finals

Continues at 1 PM this afternoon

The third Middle School Sports Meet was held yesterday at Jiaotong University in Xujiahui. Twenty-seven schools participated in the track and field events, thirty-seven schools in the group exercises, and the maneuvers reached a total of more than 2,700 people. Although the venue is located in the western corner of Shanghai, the number of spectators who took time to watch was no less than the grand occasion at Rue du Père Robert. The meeting opened at 1 PM yesterday, with Director Pan delivering the opening speech and Chu Minyi making a special trip to the meeting to deliver a speech. The preliminary rounds of 50 meters, 100 meters, and the men's 400 meters for both male and female groups were all held yesterday. The finals completed four events: men's Group A shot put, men's Group B high jump, and women's Group A and B long jump. Guan Hongda of Zhengfeng Middle School in men's Group A shot put and Rong Shujian of Aiguo Girls' School and Zhu Yanqing of Wusong in women's Group B long jump broke the previous records. The men's high hurdles and 1,500-meter preliminary round were postponed to today due to insufficient time yesterday. The details are as follows:

A Glimpse of the Venue

The main entrance of the entire venue is on Gordon Road. The order inside the venue was maintained by Nanyang Model Middle School and the Home Guard. Yesterday the weather was clear and sunny, and the athletes from each school were full of energy. The north, south, and east sides of the venue were the seating areas for each school, and various flags fluttered in the wind, dazzlingly. The rostrum was set up on the east side of the venue, displaying various prizes, which were dazzling and beautiful. On the left and right sides of the rostrum, there was a pair of antithetical couplets: "Defending the country ultimately depends on youth; Creating heroes depends on the times; Merit lies in repeated efforts," and "Advocating martial arts to strengthen the Chinese race; Sharpening the spirit through sports; The spirit inspires all people." The athletes from each school wore different uniforms with beautiful styles. The Jiaotong University track and field venue is large, but the surrounding space is relatively small, causing overcrowding of spectators and making it difficult to maintain order.

Opening Ceremony

At 1 PM, the opening ceremony was held. The track and field athletes from each school lined up in front of the track in front of the stage in order, led by the Public Security Bureau military band, followed by the meeting officials, then the female school athletes, and finally the male school athletes. They circled the field once in the melodious sound of military music, then stood in front of the stage and performed the ceremony. First, Chairman Pan Gongzhan delivered the opening speech, and also delivered a speech on behalf of Mayor Wu. Then, Yu Zhongbiao, a representative of the Municipal Party Department, Chu Minyi, the honorary advisor, and Li Zhaohuan delivered speeches in succession. Then the music was played and the ceremony was completed. The sports meeting song was sung under the guidance of Zhong Zitou, and then the students from each school entered the field for the maneuvers, with Shao Rugan giving the order and Shen Xian demonstrating.

Chairman's Speech: Chairman Pan Gongzhan's opening speech briefly stated that the significance of promoting sports at the opening of today's Third Middle School Sports Meet is not for a small number of students to compete for championships, but to encourage all students to pay attention to the dangers facing the country and the nation, and to build a good foundation for the future of the nation by strengthening their bodies. Seventy-one schools and 909 athletes participated in this year's track and field competition. More than 30 schools and 37 sections participated in group exercises, and 35 schools and 2,700 people participated in the maneuvers. Four girls' physical education schools and 45 athletes participated in the performance, which is more than in previous years. It is hoped that it will progress year by year in the future, so that physical education can be popularized to all students in the school.

Mr. Chu's Speech: Mr. Chu Minyi's speech briefly stated that he was very happy to participate in the third Shanghai Middle School Joint Sports Meet today. Chinese sports have gradually developed in recent years, and sports meets are held everywhere. However, the meaning of the sports meet is not to train a small number of athletes, but to enable every student to participate in sports, and to extend it beyond the school so that everyone can pay attention to physical education. Middle school students are in the period of proper physical development. If they are not trained during the middle school period, they will develop bad habits. Therefore, the significance of the middle school sports meet is even more important. In this time of national crisis, everyone should pay special attention to physical education. Intellectual and moral education must be developed from physical education. It is hoped that everyone will work harder.

Yunfei Achieves Three Victories in Three Battles 174

Yesterday, Defeated Datong with a Score of 48 to 32

Since its establishment, the Yunfei Basketball Team first defeated Jiaotong University, then defeated Mailing. Last night, by appointment, they competed against Datong University at Datong. At the start, Datong showed vigor and took the lead with a score of 4 to 3. Yunfei quickly rallied, with Liang and Chen scoring almost every shot, taking a commanding lead of 16 to 6. Unexpectedly, Datong did not show any weakness and pressed forward, scoring five consecutive goals, tying the score at 16 to 16. The first half ended with this tie. In the second half, the teams remained evenly matched for a short time. Yunfei then connected passes smoothly and scored continuously, soaring ahead. At this point, Datong struggled to keep up and appeared outmatched. The final score was 48 to 32, with Yunfei emerging victorious. The referee was Sun Hebin. Furthermore, the Yunfei team plans to schedule a match against Shanghai University next Thursday at 6 PM. They hope Shanghai University will contact their team.

Attention Sports Instructors and Athletes 176

To improve your athletic skills, quickly read "Diligent Sports Monthly"

"Diligent Sports Monthly" is published by the Diligent Sports Monthly Office at 392 Route Pére Robert, Shanghai. The writers are all national sports experts, such as Hao Gengsheng, Shen Tongliang, Ma Yuehan, Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, Wu Zheng, Cheng Dengke, Song Ruhai, Wang Fudan, Jiang Xiangqing, Wu Bangwei, Chen Baiqing, Shao Rugan, Shang Rumei, Chen Kuisheng, and more than one hundred others. It has been published for a year and is popular throughout the country. After the publication of Volume 2, Number 1, more than 10,000 copies have been sold. The content is rich in text and illustrations, introducing new sports theories, researching athletic techniques, and recording world and national sports news. It is an essential publication for middle and primary school sports instructors and athletes. The annual subscription for twelve issues is only two yuan. Domestic subscribers do not pay postage, while foreign subscribers add 2.2 yuan. To commemorate the anniversary, new subscribers are being sought with great enthusiasm. Currently, the Shanghai Municipal First Sports Field has invited Fu Baolu to perform the pole vault, postponed to December 1st at 2 PM. The society offers preferential treatment to subscribers, predicting Mr. Fu's performance results. Therefore, the deadline has also been extended. Those who subscribe for the entire year before the end of November can predict Mr. Fu's performance results. The first prize winner will receive a scholarship of 300 yuan, the second prize 200 yuan, and the third prize 50 yuan. Other winners will receive sports equipment, art watches, or books, with no one leaving empty-handed. In addition to the prizes, four issues of the Chinese National Sports Association's sports quarterly, worth 1.2 yuan, will also be given. Those who study sports should not miss this opportunity.

Overseas Chinese Primary and Secondary Schools Temporarily Exempt from Joint Examinations 186

The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission sent a letter to the Ministry of Education proposing that before the regulations for student graduation joint examinations in overseas Chinese primary and secondary schools are promulgated, all primary and secondary schools should be temporarily exempt from joint examinations. The Ministry of Education stated that it had previously received a request from overseas consuls to exempt schools from joint examinations before the regulations were formulated and had already issued an order to temporarily exempt them. The letter from the commission concerned the same matter as before, and it could be handled accordingly.

Review Meeting on Methods for Repairing the Confucius Temple and Forest 187

The Ministry of Education Expressed Dissent on Adding a Surcharge to Diplomas

In order to commemorate Confucius, the central government has resolved to repair the Confucius Temple and Forest in Qufu. The central government will provide a one-time subsidy of 200,000 yuan for repairs. The remaining funds are planned to be raised through two types of apportionment methods: (1) A surcharge will be added to the diplomas of students in universities, colleges, and schools: one yuan for each graduation certificate from specialized schools and above, five jiao for high school, two jiao for junior high school, and five fen for primary school; (2) The apportionment method for the tomb of Sun Yat-sen will be followed, with each provincial government being apportioned 260,000 yuan for large provinces, 150,000 yuan for medium-sized provinces, and 50,000 yuan for poor and small provinces. The resolution on this apportionment method was submitted to the Executive Yuan to order the Ministries of Interior, Education, and Finance to consult and verify before submitting it to the central government for a decision. At 9 AM the day before yesterday, the Executive Yuan convened representatives from the three ministries to meet at the Yuan to review the plan for repairing the Confucius Temple and Forest. Lu Xirong from the Ministry of Interior, Zhang Jiong from the Ministry of Education, and He Yimin from the Ministry of Finance attended, along with Teng Gu and Liang Dong from the Executive Yuan. Representative Zhang Jiong from the Ministry of Education reported on the difficulties of adding a surcharge to student graduation certificates and expressed dissent. The reasons were: (1) It is a form of arbitrary taxation and miscellaneous charges; (2) According to current statistics on the number of graduates from universities, colleges, and schools, only over 190,000 yuan can be collected annually, and it must be collected by local educational administrative agencies. The amount is small and sufficient to affect the efficiency of educational administration. Therefore, it was decided on the spot, "Regarding the cost of repairing the Confucius Temple and Forest, an estimated budget should first be prepared based on actual needs, and then an apportionment method should be proposed based on the number required in the estimated budget. The central government should first hire architectural experts to go to Qufu with representatives from the Shandong Provincial Government to conduct a survey, make accurate estimates, and construct in phases according to their urgency, prepare an estimated budget, and then discuss the apportionment method according to actual needs."

Director Pan Youqiang Reviewed the Fudan Student Army Yesterday 191

Disciplined Military Bearing and Orderly Steps

Director's Encouraging Remarks

The Ministry of Training and Supervision sent Pan Youqiang, director of the National Military Education Department, to Shanghai to review the military training results of major middle schools and universities in the city, as reported in various newspapers. Yesterday, Director Pan, accompanied by Jiao Jihua, director of the Shanghai Military Training Association, and Jiao Zhijian and Zhu Shijing from the Ministry of Training and Supervision, went to Jiangwan Fudan University to review the school's entire student army. The result was exceptionally satisfactory. The details are recorded below:

Participants: In addition to Director Pan, those who participated in the review that day also included Li Denghui, president of Fudan University, and Chen Bingde, director of the school's physical education department. Those who were reviewed were more than 800 students in the entire Fudan student army, totaling four companies. Their uniforms were neat, and their military bearing was extremely disciplined.

Review Situation: At 8 AM, Director Pan arrived at the school amidst the uplifting sound of military music and immediately inspected the area. The review began, including various movements such as formation drills, unarmed combat, and rifle exercises.

Director's Speech: After the review was completed, Director Pan began his speech. He first deeply praised the students' spirit and neat uniforms. He then discussed the bad habits of some people and finally elaborated on the importance of national military education, detailing the revival of Germany after being crushed by Napoleon, the strength of Italy in recent decades, and the recent rising national power of Russia, all due to their emphasis on military education. After Mr. Pan's speech, President Li of the school expressed his gratitude to Mr. Pan.

Further News: The Shanghai Military Education Training Department, considering that Fudan has nearly a thousand students receiving military training and that it is necessary to increase the number of educators, has reached an agreement with President Li of the school to send an additional instructor to the school in the near future.

Little Western Paradise 192

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter Four: A Cup of Water Reveals the Difficulty of Seeking Help; A Poor Worker Protects the Elderly; Ten Thousand Gold Can Be Obtained; A Cunning Official Forms a Group

These conversations were quietly overheard for a long time under the eaves by Zhang Jiefu and Li Shilian. Some of the words were heard very clearly. Some of the words were not very clear. However, the waiter's last words that the girl was also a pitiful person, and what Zhiqian said about you being a matchmaker, were all heard word for word. It was also said that the old worker would bring something to the girl. Zhang Jiefu whispered to Li Shilian with a smile: He wants to marry that girl, and he is very qualified, only he has that spare money. Li Shilian said: That's natural, the eyes of the people in the world are all bright. He sees that the person is someone who interacts with the director of the hall and the provincial committee, so naturally he wants to curry favor in that direction. Zhang Jiefu said: Mr. Li's letters, have they all been sent? I think you are a shrewd and capable person, and your future must be very promising. When Li Shilian heard someone praising him, he looked very proud, raised his eyebrows, and smiled: That's hard to say. Zhang Jiefu saw his appearance, he was a little conceited, and he couldn't help feeling ashamed that he didn't have the confidence to find a job. He put his hands behind his back and wandered around under the eaves. Li Shilian thought, his attitude is saying that I am bragging. When I have a chance, I will show off to him. So he shouted: Waiter, come, hire me a rickshaw to the Ministry of Finance. When Zhang Jiefu heard this, he glared at him but didn't say anything. When the waiter heard that he was going to the Ministry of Finance, it seemed that he was also getting a little bit of noble air, and he answered with a very crisp voice. So Li Shilian went back to his room to put on a mandarin jacket, put on his hat, came out, nodded to Zhang Jiefu and said: See you later. Zhang Jiefu smiled: Are you going to see Director Qian at the Ministry of Finance? Li Shilian puffed out his chest, buttoned the buttons on his chest and said: I'm going to try my luck, but I'm not sure. With that, he flicked his sleeves and walked out the door. When he arrived at the gate, the rickshaw hired by the waiter was already waiting in front of the door. The rickshaw puller asked: Sir, are you going to the Ministry of Finance? Li Shilian looked back, and answered in a low voice: I'm not going to the Ministry of Finance, pull me to Nan Yuan Men to buy something. (60)

There is No One in China 193

— By Yishi

By chance, I met several Western friends. Whenever we met, we always had a good time talking and laughing. Because they have lived in China for many years, they can speak Shanghai dialect fluently. From then on, I began to pay attention to their actions, and sometimes I tried to test their patriotic personality.

Once in the park, we met unexpectedly, what a joy! To be in such a poetic and picturesque garden, and to be able to talk and laugh with each other, is such an interesting thing?

"Yi, are there no people in your country?" The most mischievous one, named J.K., usually likes to joke with people, this time he asked me like this right away.

"Haha! J.K., you are too naughty, we have 450 million compatriots, how can there be no one?" I was very surprised, and at the same time I was wondering if what he said contained a sarcastic meaning.

"Sigh! Yi, you are lying again, there are obviously no people in your country."

... Silence, hesitation stirred in my heart.

"Hey! Let me ask you, can anyone in your country manufacture weapons?"

"No."

"Can anyone in your country manufacture trains?"

"No."

"Can anyone in your country manufacture airplanes?"

"No." (The fourth one is still no)

"Then isn't there no one in your country?"

"Um..."

At that time, after hearing these words, my chest was filled with boundless grief and indignation, and I felt a burning sensation in my heart. Everyone was stunned for a while before parting.

Thank you to this friend for giving me an opportunity to reflect, and at the same time, I would like to encourage a group of passionate youths.

Tidbits 194

— (Qinfang)

The chirping of crickets. It's like self-destructive heroes congratulating themselves. But now your end has come.
